4. ( Complete ) [* 5 *] Chop Tree Not solved this reboot.
There is a tree hidden in newbie land and you need an axe to chop it down.
This time the tree was hidden in disney behind Donalds house. Axe was in
a tree in hidden area west of weary pesant in farmland, entrance is footpath.
Tree was hidden in newbie forest last time through newbie land.

5. ( Complete ) [* 5 *] Codename: Kodiak Not solved this reboot.
Search rubble in one north room and you'll find a secret area over it.
You will find an elevator in there search elevator and enter it.
Search floor and Ceiling. Talk to Ford and he will give you password.
Give password to Richardson and he will give you a helmet.
Wear the helmet and scan every room. When the helmet says 75% search room.
Their will be an secret exit. Next room will be Kodiak. Kill him!

7. ( Complete ) [* 5 *] Mack Not solved this reboot.
Mack is a hidden exix, a block in the middle of nowhere. Search block.
Get a donut and give to duplocop and he give you a key. Unlock and enter
cell and search wall. Get a combo for lock box. Go to bank and request
that number. Get block from box. Go get ladder and enter duploschool
kill teacher search black board. Get bone. Give bone to duplodog and 
he digs up block get block. Attach block to block and it makes a key.
He south to a house and go to the attic. Go up, unlock door, kill Mack.

16. ( Complete ) [* 10*] Disney Not solved this reboot.
Go to the west until you can go south. Then go all south and all west 
until you find Doc at the mine. Say diamond and he'll give you a pickaxe.
Swing pickaxe in every room of the mine until you find the diamond, 
then go back to where you went south. Head all west to the house in 
the forest and go in. Give the diamond to Snow White and say mirror. 
She'll give you a mirror. Go all e from the beginning until you can 
swim, swim, go first s, kill ursula, s, get letter, go back to witch, 
show letter to witch, talk to witch until she says she wants the mirror, 
show mirror to witch, give mirror to witch.plan She drops the award, 
pick it up and go back to the mirror. Head south and check out the 
first house to the west. Inside is Mickey, give the award to him.


17. ( Not Done ) [ 10 ] Djinni Not solved this reboot.
Djinni: Djinni Bring a light source.
Wayhaven, all e, leave, folow road e/ne until you get to the docks. 
In the room before either dock (exits e or n) swim or swim in ocean.
Swim until you get to another beach with only exit south. 
Go s and then climb over rocks then examine cliff, examine 
cave etc. Dive water, watch mob until it settles on the bottom, 
kill mob, examine bottom, search slime, get bottle. 
(Key you get from mob can be used to open a tan box on 
the island in this area to get a tan marble).

Once you 
have the bottle, return home or to a good area. 
You may want to put eq in a box as you can't use 
eq or guild powers once inside the bottle.
Remove cork.

You now suck. I will only say the 
things you have to do - you may want to kill the
mobs to get eq as you will have none.
Go to the room with Stinky/Skippy/whatever his name is
- he is the newbie. 
Here you can pick flowers for a 100 hp heal. 
Left of him is a room with an anorexic slave. 
You can exa garden, pick vegetables, get vegetables.
Each vegetable gives approx 100 hp heal. You will need these!
Go to the mage, wait until he says the magic word 'Kazam' 
To the right of the mage, search rocks for a hunting knife, 
this helps ALOT! Go to centre and say key in front of a mob 
(I did this with the rogue but I assume it will work for any of them).
Mob will tell you which little mob in the outer circle has their particular key.
Go to them and say key again. 
They will give you a key to the door.
Kill guard in inner circle (I found him pretty hard), 
unlock door, go 2n - here is the mage (non-aggro) 
I would suggest having as many flowers/vegetables and ppl available 
for hmheal from afar as possible for this bit.
Kill mage, get sword. Go s, search room, say kazam, 
climb stairs, give sword to Djinni. (10)

29. ( Complete ) [ 15 ] Alphabet Not solved this reboot.
Chaos/enter/2e/d. Kill the letters to spell the word HELICOPTER. 
You only need one E. Make sure you have one of the items other than a 
letter from one of the kills. The letter R is in a hidden room. 
Once you have all this, go back to the H room and 'spell helicopter'. 
Note that if you leave the area for any reason before you spell helicopter
that you have to do it all over again.

exa staff
A branch of wood as white as purest ivory, this short staff is decorated and
inscribed with designs formed by orange sand and turquoise jelly. The origin
of these strange and serpentine images is truly not of the present realm. It
appears to be more an object of divinity, than a weapon for combat.
This weapon is in excellent condition.
exa designs
The images on the staff appear to be totally disordered at first. As
you gaze closer, you begin to see patterns emerge from the chaos. 
Suddenly, as if your mind and eyes are focusing in unison for the first
time, the majesty of the overall design becomes clear. You are
awestricken by the power bound up in this staff and fear what might
happen if the pattern was traced and the power unleashed. 
trace pattern
As you trace the pattern on the staff, bright sparks of
white light dance around in your wake. Surges of energy
course through your body; almost more than you can bear!
You almost give up in agony, when suddenly, you finish.
The staff is definitely warmer, but there doesn't seem to
have been any apocalyptic, or even interesting, results.
You look around, half in disappointment, half in anticipation.
The quarterstaff warms to your grasp.
The quarterstaff warms to your grasp.
The staff abruptly turns cold!
The hoary, freezing sensation becomes almost unbearable --
it feels more blistering than the breath of a red dragon,
yet you are unable to loosen your grip!
The artifact suddenly bursts into flame, an icy white 
conflagration which envelops your hand, and soon your
entire arm!
The silver blaze consumes your shoulder, your torso...unable
even to think, you watch with awe and dread as your entire body
is soon indistinguishable from the flame itself!
A deafening clap of energy resounds forth from within your body!
Another burst of searing sound, as though a barrier were
being razed! 
Three more blasts of deafening proportions, in quick succession!
You can see nothing around you except a light beyond that of the sun!
...then, silence...the deepest depths of silence, a state
beyond peace...
...at the center of your vision, barely outlined by a soft aura of
white light, you see a shape...you cannot discern whether the
image exists in space before you, or in your very mind...
As you gaze at the figure, you find yourself thinking the 
following words:
'I must move to the center of my world...'
'...once there, I must look up, towards the sky...'
'...at that time, I will begin to understand.'
The image fades, and as the light surrounding it dies down,
you sense that the moment has ended...
The artifact, once burned into your hand, has disappeared.
Sight returns to your eyes, darkness becomes light again.
COT
look up
You turn your gaze skyward, and fix your eyes upon the world above...
...the multicolored sky appears as it always does, but gradually...
...shapes in the sky begin to become apparent to you...the pompous
clouds gently round their edges and project sinews of mist in the
vague suggestion of...faces!
...and these faces, these half-realities that seem to exist partly
in your very mind, begin to assume the countenances of men...
...shifting your gaze about, you notice that the entire sky, the
limitless expanse a horizon around, is alive with these faces,
expressions of the very essence of peace...
...a slim, blue face floats in front of a wide, indigo face, both
smiling upon you as though you were an honored visitor to their
reality......seemingly swimming in the molasses of the infinite space, these 
benevolent profiles collectively close their eyes towards you,
and you feel a slight shiver budding from inside your heart...
...you glance down in a momentary response towards the subtle
pain in your chest -- it is both a pain of envy and of bliss...
...as you quickly raise your eyes back up to the skies, still
cowering slightly over your heart, you see that the faces have
gone, slipped back into the hilts and scabbards of the clouds 
and constellations...
...you are left with the vague knowledge that there exists a
dimension of life far above this one, where thoughts pass as
though silent lightning through the clouds, and where a bliss
may be found amongst the brash spirits of the wind and rain.

of the sky are no more, and Sightless is yours.

56. ( Complete ) [ 30 ] Shadowrun Not solved this reboot.
Shadowrun: First: map Atlanta (in science) otherwise you'll get lost.
Find Mr Johnson in Atlanta. He is located 2w, 2n, 2w from the subway 
entrance.

Speak to him about the quest, then follow these steps:


1. First, get the door remover in the gunshop on the south end of 
Avery Street by killing the guy in the 2nd room. (subway, 1w, 9s, 2w).


2. Activate the remover in the activator 5n and 4e, d from the subway 
entrance.

3. Go to the green lightning gang hideout (1w, 7s, 3e, s) 
and remove the door that is 2 south and up from the entrance. Kill 
the leader for the passcard. He is 47k, but only has one attack.

4. 
Activate the passcard in the activator in the north east corner of town.
From the subway, 4n, 6e, 2n, e, s.

5. The go down to the parking garage
(2e, n from subway) and go down to the 5th sublevel. In the northwest 
corner of the 5th level insert passcard.

6. Enter and kill the drone.
It will die easily. Go past it and get the datachip. Then get out 
of the garage. 

7. Go and activate the datachip in the 3rd activator, 
which you have not used yet. It is located 7e from the subway. 
Then go and give the activated datachip to Mr. Johnson in the bar 
in the northwest part of town.
He will give you 10k coins and the qps.. (30)

96. ( Not Done ) [ 100 ] Ravenloft Not solved this reboot.Qinfo (last updated 12/12/98)
The majority of these are written from memory so the exact syntax might not be included. While there are directions for some of the quests, THERE ARE NO MAPS. Those of us who did the quests on our own had to map and explore...SO SHALL YOU. This is good for you because if you go through like a laundry list you WILL get popped for qinfo. Numbers that aren't listed have been removed from the game. Special thanks to all the people who helped by providing information on quests I haven't done. No names (for security reasons), but you know who you are. Whenever possible I've added notes about possible death traps and toughness of mobs. 

1) Marbles: these are found all over the mud. See Marble List. (1qp each)
2) Tree: from cot: s/2e/2s/look at tree. (5)
4) Resource Crisis: newbie land, find the mirror with the oil field in it. Search behind the seat of the truck. In the tool shed, in the office desk and just everywhere. You need a digital multimeter and a pair of wire clippers. Then, after you have those, find the tower you can climb up. There's a device. Test each wire with the multimeter. The one with the charge is the one you need to clip. (5)
5) Newbie Academy: from newbie bin, go s, d, n and enroll in the school. Answer all the questions, they answers are all in help files and room descriptions. Make sure you know the phone number to the White House. If you aren't a newbie, you can still do this quest. In the sewers of Pinnacle look for the newbie mice and you're on your way. (5)
6) Mack: find the duploland mirror in newbie land. Find the bone somewhere in there. You'll have to search around. Give it to the dog, he'll give you a piece of a key. Buy a donut and give it to the duplocop. Go into the jail cell and find the password (C1FB as far as I know). Take it to the bank and ask the teller for the box. In it is the other half of the key. Find the stepladder and go to the house and find the trapdoor leading up. Go up, n, unlock door, open door, w and kill Mack. (5)
7) Free Cho: chaos/enter/4w/e/s/e. you need to activate the machine by pulling levers flipping switches, pushing buttons, etc. Kill all the mobs you see in there. Careful, as this is no wimpy. After you kill all of them, eventually you'll see Dr. Cho. Type 'free Cho' and finish killing the mobs. Then you're done! (5)
8) Codename Kodiak: in newbie land, find the battletech mirror and go in. go nw/nw/e/nw/nw/nw and go into the elevator shaft. Go up and talk to the guy. Then, go back down into the elevator, and then search the boards. Go down and talk to the guy there, he'll give you a helmet. Wear the helmet and go u/se/se/se/w/se/sw/se/sw/and search trees. You'll see a hidden exit ONLY if you wear the helmet. Go kill Kodiak. (5)
9) Chop Tree: you need an axe and some patience for this one. Search all the rooms in each of the mirrors with your trusty axe. You'll find an old oak tree. When you find it, just type 'chop tree' and you're done. (5)
10) Bug: No qinfo for this one. The mosquito flies around pinnacle and everyone is free to attack it. It can take massive amounts of damage, so dedicate some time for this. It will randomly leave to another place in Pinnacle, and might just port you somewhere else randomly. Only problem I can find is getting it after it's gone into the cemetery. (5)
11) Bbn Planet: chaos/2w/lift manhole cover/n/kill tech (5k)/search wall/kill tech (5k)/plug DCR.NET cable into lower server (5)
12) Zetron: Fantasy/city portal. Go 2n/w/enter stall and buy a medium sized ladder. Go 3 or 4 east from that stall and enter the next one and buy incense. Go to the portal and search portal, retrieve seal. Then go 7w/6s/3w/s and find the shrine to Zetron. Burn incense, pray, return seal. (10)
14) Spaceport: chaos/enter/2n/w/u/board shuttle/pull lever like 4 times. Go to the desert and find the fremen. Kill them and get the comb. Comb desert. Go n from there and blow up the death star and kill the emperor. Get his heart. Then find the statue and search the statue. Go inside the little gift shop thing and buy an amulet/medallion. Go back out to the statue and practice on it. Or raise statue. I don't recall, but toy around with it. Then go s to where there's a creature. Kill Vader and get HIS heart. Go back to yoda and give the 2 hearts to yoda. (10)
15) Save Grandma: chaos/all s/ne. You'll be in a forest. Search every room for a red cloak. Wear the cloak and go to the house in the northeast corner. Knock on door. Kill the wolf and open closet. (10)
16) Sarkath Khan: fantasy/city portal/12n/leave/8n/5w/2n/path/enter. Order room/order beer/sit/give beer to zarkoff. Listen to his story, go upstairs, and then sleep in your room. Then look at the map and go to the cave. Inside the cave go n, ne, nw and kill the mobs. Open the coffin once they're dead and 'free Sarkath khan' (10)
17) Rampart: fantasy/city portal/15e/exit/16e/2s/sinkhole. Pray, accept_challenge, the answers are compassion, heart, mind, forgiveness, understanding, love. Go out, and get back to the sinkhole. Give soulgem to figure. (10)
18) NY Mugger: science/enter/u/2e/d/board train. When you get to NY wander around till you find the mugger and kick his fucking ass! (10)
19) Nightmare: chaos/enter/w/7n/w/n/search bed/sleep in bed. Find the classroom (all e/all s). From there you need to get the following: box of chocolates (tray in cafeteria), art (art room), love letter (locker), binaca blast (principal), gift (bully's jacket pocket). Then go all n/e/s to your ideal mate. Give them all to her except the blast. Push button to get a minty breath. Kiss her (10)
20) Lothlarian: This has changed. The only info I have for the new way is this: enter mirror/s/search trees/w/s/w/w/s/s/w kill the three Phoenix Guards then go north. Kill general then search papers several times until is says something about the shrubs being the weak point of the defenses/e/n/search shrubs/n/e/n/e/e/s/s/s/skill ghost and enter fort. n/n/n/d/enter darkness kill arkhan and get standard. nw/u/s/s/out/n/n/n/n/w/w/s/w/s raise standard. This will only work if you're evil. (10)
21) Gameshow: chaos/enter/2e/all n. This one is random, and there are a few gameshows. The ones it can be are price is right, wheel of fortune, and $10,000 pyramid. To get to the pyramid you have to go to family feud, get to the final round, kill Richard Dawson and search wall. Price is right you just go in, kill bob barker, kill contestant, and spin the wheel. Common answer on WoF is 'Cancer the tradesman', though this changes. (10)
22) Djinni: fantasy/city portal/all e/leave/all e/4n/2e/look at water/swim in ocean/ocean/look for the se corner or thereabouts. You'll have to go east about 10 times before it puts you on an island. Search sand until you find a bottle. Open the bottle and you get sucked in, becoming a newbie with NOTHING until you finish it or leave. Find the guard, kill him, get his stuff, and enter the palace. Climb the stairs and find the Djinni. Go back down, north. Kill the guy and get the sword from him. Go back upstairs and give it to the Djinni. (10)
23) Disney: find the mirror that has the small coastal town in it. Go to the west until you can go south. Then go all south and all west until you find Doc at the mine. Say diamond and he'll give you a pickaxe. Swing pickaxe in every room of the mine until you find the diamond, then go back to where you went south. Head all west to the house in the forest and go in. Give the diamond to Snow White and say mirror. She'll give you a mirror, then go out and give the mirror to the old woman. She drops the award, pick it up and go back to the mirror. Head south and check out the first house to the west. Inside is Mickey, give the award to him. (10)
24) Destroy Barney: Chaos/enter/w/all s/all e/n. This has been changed. As soon as I figure it out... (10)
25) Arcanarton: Fantasy/road portal. Go south and all west until you find an exit leading sw. Go sw and you'll be at the tower. Go up the tower to the very top, where you'll find Arcanarton. Careful of the followers. They're about 20k aggro and four in a room can hit you for over 200 points of damage in a single round. Arcanarton is at the top, 30k-35k, non-aggro, non-hunting wimpy safe. Kill him. There is also a marble here (see marble list for details). (10)
26) Perfection: Chaos/enter/4w/e/s/w/s/2e/n. Enter warehouse/tease flower/kill tulip/kill nail/get everything/enter imperfect panel/kiss glass/lick film/ride particles/tease flower/enter imperfect panel/qwerty/lick film/ride particles/tussle flower/kill nail/kill tulip/get nothing/taste experience/conduct experiment/caress tulips/be perfect/do nothing/tease flower/enter perfect panel/up/enter heart/die/return nothing/somewhere/tussle flower/taste experience/climb ladder/return everything. You're on your own to get out. I found that if you reverse some of the above steps you eventually get back out. (12)
28) Hobgoblin: Fantasy/city portal/12n/leave/all n. Take the path and enter the cave. Go all north once inside to the stream. Jump over stream and search the bones. Go back and head west till you can go up. Go up and kill the kid with knife. Get the knife. Go back down twice and head south to find the crazy hobgoblin. Give the knife and the bone to him and he gives you a flute. Go west and find the hobgoblin priest. Play flute and the priest will die. Get the amulet and leave. Go back to the city portal and go 7 west and then south. Search around near the Shrine to Zetron for the Tower of Zalusta. Enter the tower, say Zalusta, go all up, go south and give the amulet to Zalusta. (15)
29) Alphabet: Chaos/enter/2e/d. Kill the letters to spell the word HELICOPTER. You only need one E. Make sure you have one of the items other than a letter from one of the kills. The letter R is in a hidden room. Once you have all this, go back to the H room and 'spell helicopter'. Note that if you leave the area for any reason before you spell helicopter that you have to do it all over again. (15)
30) Waldo: Chaos/enter/4w/2e/w. You should be in Waldo's house. Find the closet and search around. You'll find a hole on the shelf. Type 'in' to go through it. Walk like Waldo. When you see the real Waldo, say waterworld and shake his hand. (20)

51) Miyu: This is the only one I'm providing a map for. Look for a boy wandering around chaos. look at him, type: trace symbol, and you're in the Miyu area. Map of Kyoto: 
*-*-*-*-T 
|
I *
| | 
*-A *
| | *=just a room
*-*-*-* S=Start 
| | H=House entrance
* * * L=Library 
| | A=Armour 
*-*-*-L T=temple 
| I=Inn
H-*-*-*
|
* 
| 
*-S-*
The directions to this area take a while to get used to: they aren't n, s, e, w. Instead it uses left, right, forwards, backwards, and the orientation depends totally from what direction you entered the room from. You'll get used to it. Go to H on the map. Search houses, enter house. Once inside house, search debris. You'll find a mirror, which the boy in the house will take. Kill boy, get mirror. Also look at the picture on the wall here. Go out, and go to L on the map. Search the records, and you find a diary. Kill the boy here (he takes the diary before you can).Read the diary.. it gives some history to the quest. Go to T.. this is where the vampire Miyu is. Go back one space from her. Drop all your gear. Then go back into the temple. Say hi, and she asks if she can bite you. Say yes, then type: bite me. She bites you, and reduces you to 1 hp. When she bites you, she also makes you drop everything you were carrying, and she takes it. This is why you drop your stuff i!
!
n the other room. Heal yourself. get your gear, and then go to the Armor (marked A on map). Look at the mirror. Use mirror. Type: use mirror on armor. Then kill the armor. This armor is tough... but you can't kill it at all unless you use the mirror on it first, and have been bitten by Miyu. When Armor is dead, sever head from corpse. get head. Go back to H, enter house, place head in picture. (40)

Go down and the Gnome Warlord is east (he's major trouble. Get help killing him). Get the amulet from his backpack. Go back to the oil painting and go north. Move the grate and you end up in a maze. Map it. By wearing the gnome's amulet most of the other gnomes will let you pass. Kill the dragon and get the key, then go se and search dung. Go d/3e/s/e/n/e/2s/3e/s/3w/s/2e/s/2w/s. You can't go back north. Continue 3e/n/e/s/e and unlock the door, then go north and kill the Minotaur. Get the crystal from him. Go s/w/n/w/s/2w/search and climb cleft. r one. Leave the massage parlor, go back s, sw, s, se, s, se, then go: sw, 2s, and into the large plaza area. Wander around here until you find a tourist with a camcorder. Kill them and get it. 64) Ring of Power: Go to the zoo in chaos. From Da Void, it's n, w, n, and then search around a bit.. it's near the hide and seek quest. Enter the zoo, go 3n into zookeeper's house. You will soon find that directions don't correspond: so that if you go left to get to one room, if you then go right you probably won't end up back where you began. So mark the rooms and work out the directions. !
!
There are 15 rooms total. When I did it, the directions to the end were: forward, forward, left, left, backwards, left, left, backwards, left, left, forward, right, forward, and you should be at castle. Don't enter the castle yet! Search stone, go down, kill dragon. Put horn in conical hole, put feather in oblong hole, put tail in cylindrical hole, get ring of power. Then go up. ite keep. Kill guards, 2n and you see a fountain. Melt ice (need that torch). Get scroll. Go ne, 2u, n, push stone (on pillar) and get black key. Go to black keep. ind a crystal key. If not search around for more nests.

Octagonal Key: The octagonal key is on a courier who wanders in the area. I have always found him in the north east section. Follow him and kill him (easy). Get octagonal key. 
When you're ready for the final assault on the palace, look at the scroll. Chant the words on the scroll and you end up at the cliff where you have to 'search cliff' and go up. Actually, this place is 7n of the portal of life, and you don't need the scroll at all to get there. Go up, n, kill lich, 2 or 3n, till you see a pillar. Unlock pillar (with crystal key) and the drawbridge comes down. Go north and into palace. The palace is basically a square, with a tower at each corner. In each tower is a device you need to unlock (using hex or octagonal key). When this happens the pyramid they were supporting floats to the ground and you can go in to free the queen.
What you do is: from just inside palace, go: w, kill cleric (no wimpy, but he's not too hard), sw, up, kill lich, (no wimpy), u, unlock device. 2d, ne, 2e, kill cleric (no wimpy), se, up, now there is a lich here who won't let you go up. Kill him, and you can go 2u, unlock device, 2d, kill lich, nw, 2n, kill cleric (no wimpy), ne, u, dispose of the lich, u, unlock device, 2d, sw, 2w (past a couple of clerics, but they allow you to wimpy), nw, u, dispose of lich, u, unlock device. Now all the devices are inactivated, and the pyramid should come down. Go 2d, se, e, kill the 2 clerics, 2s, wield the staff of the positive plane, kill cleric. He should vaporize with the first hit. Get out all 5 orbs, look at the stone, and insert orbs. When you do this, the queen is freed, and the quest is done! 
Notes: If you let the lich follow you any further than the base of the tower, then it will stop you leaving and you will have to fight it to the death. The liches take a while to kill, so they are annoying. If you have somebody as a tank in the palace, don't wield the staff of the positive plane until you have to kill the final cleric. If you are wielding the staff then monsters will attack you, even if someone is trying to defend. Blow the whistle you got from the smuggler and he'll come and take you to a secret entrance. Search the ladder (to disarm a trap). Climb up and kill the mayor. (95)

Barovia
You need to get items for Ismark to make you a shield and a helmet. When you are wearing these, you can go to the Barovia graveyard and kneel at Ismail's grave. That's all of the quest. From forest portal, go to ravenloft:2s, sw, w, nw, enter mist, kill nightmare, in. Then, go: n, nw, w, nw, search river, get stone (unique item, I think)go: 2e, ne, n, nw, n, ne, n, 2ne, 2e, 2n, w, nw, n, w, follow coffer corpse (it flees a lot :P), kill coffer corpse, get silver. go 2e (if you're still in the coffer corpse's original room), follow apparition (also flees), kill apparition, get gold. go: w, s, se, e, 2s, w, kill bats, w, kill bats. Every so often, when you kill a bat, the wings remain undamaged, and are left behind. This is what you are looking for... so keep killing bats till you get some bat wings. If you're unlucky you may have to wander the forest for a bit, till you get some. go: 2sw, 6w, 2s, nudge ismark, type: make helmet. He'll now make you a bat wing helmet to w!
!
ear. Go to ice portal in fantasy. Then go south and east until you reach a glacier where you can climb up. Cross the glacier (e,n), go down the other side, s, enter the cave in the glacier wall. Search stones, get mithril. All you need now is another block of gold but you have to wait for the Apparition to reset to get it ! :(Go back to apparition in ravenloft. Get another block of gold. When you have the block of gold, go back to Ismark (w,s,se,e,2s,2w,2sw,6w,2s) Type: make shield. Wear the shield, go back to the graveyard (2n, 5w, n, w). Kneel.

--GOBLINHEAD--O.K.....I'll start with the problem....you need to find a scroll of charm protection, cause the one monster charms you and either makes you drop all or jump off a cliff. You'll also need another person to help you get to said monster.
1) Enter fantasy portal, then go to the road portal.
2) Go into Balooga falls, 4 or 5 east of the portal I think, look for a bar to the north. go into the bar, and say forgers. (bar may be a little west or east...somewhere around the above directions is close).
3) Give 1000 coins to forger, he'll give you some I.D.
4) Go to the icy blue portal and get a ring or two of feather falling
5) Get the scroll of charm protection, I have no idea where it is, or if you can find a nice cleric who is quick enough at bouncing, they can kill the harpy without it (with a little luck and no lag)
6) Go west to the end of the road from road portal, north to the tundra, west a bit, look for a path leading north in the room descriptions, then go north.
7) Load the catapult with some junk, like bread, pull, and fire. You'll have to adjust it to fire it into the cave opening using adjust #, usually between 10 and 15. When it is firing into the cave, load yourself in the catapult and get someone to fire you in there. This is where the harpy is that will charm you.
8) Kill harpy, then kill the goblin king. sever head. take the head to the lord in the castle that is 3s and a couple west of the place where the road curves south...show I.D. to the keep guard, then enter. the lord is to the west or northwest. Look around, find him, and give him the head. he'll give you some stuff, go back to the guild and collect the quest points.

When you find it, use your card to open it, and kill the boomer,search and get neural implant (a once per reboot item). Leave the sewers, then: nw, w, nw, ne, s, ne, n, 3e, n, n, kill guards. Qinfo (last updated 04/15/03)


The majority of these are written from memory so the exact syntax might not be included. While there are directions for some of the quests, THERE ARE NO MAPS. Those of us who did the quests on our own had to map and explore...SO SHALL YOU. This is good for you because if you go through like a laundry list you WILL get popped for qinfo. Special thanks to all the people who helped by providing information on quests I haven't done. No names (for security reasons), but you know who you are. Whenever possible I've added notes about possible death traps and toughness of mobs. 

1) Marbles: these are found all over the mud. See Marble List. (1qp each)

2) Bbn Planet: chaos/2w/lift manhole cover/n/kill tech (5k)/search wall/kill tech (5k)/exa upper,middle, lower server/plug DCR.NET cable into one that is most alive (5)

3) Bug: No qinfo for this one. The mosquito flies around pinnacle and everyone is free to attack it. It can take massive amounts of damage, so dedicate some time for this. It will randomly leave to another place in Pinnacle, and might just port you somewhere else randomly. Only problem I can find is getting it after it's gone into the cemetery. (5)

4) Chop Tree: you need an axe and some patience for this one. Search all the rooms in each of the mirrors with your trusty axe. You'll find an old oak tree. When you find it, just type 'chop tree' and you're done. (5)


5) Codename Kodiak: in newbie land, find the battletech mirror and go in. go nw/nw/e/search rubble/nw/nw/nw/search doors/nw and go into the elevator shaft. Go up and talk to the guy. Then, go back down into the elevator, and then search the boards. Go down and talk to the guy there, he'll give you a helmet. Wear the helmet and go u/se/se/se/se/w/se/sw/se/sw/and search trees. You'll see a hidden exit ONLY if you wear the helmet. Go kill Kodiak. (5)


6) Free Cho: chaos/enter/4w/e/s/e. you need to activate the machine by turn knob, flip switch, press button. Kill all the mobs you see in there. Careful, as this is no wimpy. After you kill all of them, eventually you'll see Dr. Cho. Type 'free Cho', search beam to get out. Then you're done! (5)


7) Mack: newbie land. Newbie Mack: duploland:
1st- get ladder - 4w/4s/w/s/get ladder
2nd- get block #1 - buy donut/give to cop-(unlock door/open door/w/read wall(get number)) - go to bank/ask box (####)
3rd- get block #2 - enter barn/u/kill hen/search/give bone to dog 4th- kill mack-s end of house/l at ceiling/u/n/attach %% to %%/unlock door/open door/w (mack is kind of tough)

8) Newbie Academy: from newbie bin, go s, d, n and enroll in the school. Answer all the questions, they answers are all in help files and room descriptions. Make sure you know the phone number to the White House. If you aren't a newbie, you can still do this quest. In the sewers of Pinnacle look for the newbie mice and you're on your way, Science, 2w, 3n, d, n, w, 2s, 3w, 2s, 2e, 5s, u. (5)

9) Ralintaro - search around (ground and brambles and wall) for skeletons. One will have a scroll with magic words to get into the tower. Chant the words and enter and go e, exa peg/search peg, you'll find another scroll with directions to find a pen which is in the west most room. then go all north, west and kill the guardian then trace the symbol with pen and kill ralintaro. (5)

10) Resource Crisis: newbie land, find the mirror with the oil field in it. Search behind the seat of the truck. In the tool shed, in the office desk and just everywhere. You need a digital multimeter and a pair of wire clippers. Then, after you have those, find the tower you can climb up. There's a device. Test each wire with the multimeter. The one with the charge is the one you need to clip. (5)

11) REMOVED

12) Tree: from cot: s/2e/2s/look at tree. (5)



13) Twelve Princesses:

chaos, 4w, e, s, w, s, 3e, enter, nw, recline. Say hi, say king, say proclamation, say defenses, (if she doesn't give you the cloak now, drink the wine the first night then come back to her an say help), road, say hi, say yes, say daughters, say help, w, n, search each bed individually - search bed 1 etc - mine was bed 4. Go to your room, lay down, pour wine, wear cloak, go north, knock on bedpost, d, prune twig, w, prune twig, w, prune twig, board, search princesses, exa stopped couple, exa goblet, search goblet, clutch goblet, board, go back to king, give all twigs (in order) to king, give goblet to king. Done. (8)


14) Arcanarton: Fantasy/road portal/2w/s/sw/trail/enter. 
Go up the tower to the very top, where you'll find Arcanarton.
Arcanarton is at the top, 30k-35k, non-aggro, non-hunting wimpy safe.
Kill him. There is also a marble here (see marble list for details).
(10)


15) Destroy Barney: Chaos/enter/w/3s/3e/n, enter. kill the stagehand to get his pass, he moves around, so find him as you make your way towards barney. go e, 2n, search box, take liquor, 2w, 3s, 3w, show pass, search couch, give bottle to barney. (10)


16) Disney: find the mirror that has the small coastal town in it. Go to the west until you can go south. Then go all south and all west until you find Doc at the mine. Say diamond and he'll give you a pickaxe. Swing pickaxe in every room of the mine until you find the diamond, then go back to where you went south. Head all west to the house in the forest and go in. Give the diamond to Snow White and say mirror. She'll give you a mirror. Go all e from the beginning until you can swim, swim, go first s, kill ursula, s, get letter, go back to witch, show letter to witch, talk to witch until she says she wants the mirror, show mirror to witch, give mirror to witch.plan She drops the award, pick it up and go back to the mirror. Head south and check out the first house to the west. Inside is Mickey, give the award to him. (10)


17) Djinni: Djinni Bring a light source.
Wayhaven, all e, leave, folow road e/ne until you get to the docks. 
In the room before either dock (exits e or n) swim or swim in ocean.
Swim until you get to another beach with only exit south. 
Go s and then climb over rocks then examine cliff, examine 
cave etc. Dive water, watch mob until it settles on the bottom, 
kill mob, examine bottom, search slime, get bottle. 
(Key you get from mob can be used to open a tan box on 
the island in this area to get a tan marble).

Once you 
have the bottle, return home or to a good area. 
You may want to put eq in a box as you can't use 
eq or guild powers once inside the bottle.
Remove cork.

You now suck. I will only say the 
things you have to do - you may want to kill the
mobs to get eq as you will have none.
Go to the room with Stinky/Skippy/whatever his name is
- he is the newbie. 
Here you can pick flowers for a 100 hp heal. 
Left of him is a room with an anorexic slave. 
You can exa garden, pick vegetables, get vegetables.
Each vegetable gives approx 100 hp heal. You will need these!
Go to the mage, wait until he says the magic word 'Kazam' 
To the right of the mage, search rocks for a hunting knife, 
this helps ALOT! Go to centre and say key in front of a mob 
(I did this with the rogue but I assume it will work for any of them).
Mob will tell you which little mob in the outer circle has their particular key.
Go to them and say key again. 
They will give you a key to the door.
Kill guard in inner circle (I found him pretty hard), 
unlock door, go 2n - here is the mage (non-aggro) 
I would suggest having as many flowers/vegetables and ppl available 
for hmheal from afar as possible for this bit.
Kill mage, get sword. Go s, search room, say kazam, 
climb stairs, give sword to Djinni. (10)

Give the knife and the bone to him and he gives you a flute. Go west and find the hobgoblin priest. Play flute and the priest will die. Get the amulet and leave. 38) Accipiter: (25) 
Accipiter says: Ahh, good, good...you are most kind. There is a special forest south of the mainland, the Forest of Types. If only you'd be so kind as to retrieve for me a branch of the Moon Tree, and some Turquoise Jelly. Accipiter says: Turquoise Jelly is a useful ooze congealed from the branch sap of a water tree. Some shamans value it in rain-making spells. I myself use it in some recipes for its light,salty flavour.
Accipiter continues: It is a trifling request almost... both are easily enough obtained. And I will ensure that the forest will aid you.

Accipiter says: I need both items for a broth I am cooking. When you return with them, we can both sit and enjoy the warm soup,and I'll tell you all you wish to know about the world of the creators.
Accipiter says: Oh, and concern yourself not with the crane who guards my home... he will pay you no heed.
Accipiter says: The Forest of Types is an enchanting island to the south,and a fairly new addition to our realms. Its origins have a tale about them...
You say: tale
Accipiter says: Several centuries past, back when the realms were lush, untorn by the new beasts called into our lands whilst their summoners waged a bitter, pointless struggle, our kind was born.
Accipiter says: As it was told to our first generation, and as it has been passed down through our myths and blood, our own war would be with the man/trees of the north. And yea, for centuries we did war with the trees, as it continues today thus.
Accipiter says: However, once a young hawk named Accipiter came of age, he decided that blood need not be spilt any longer, that our claws need not sunder bark, nor our beaks pierce the dry flesh of wood any more.
Accipiter says: This young hawk was the first to voice such a thought, and he was received thus with indifference at first. However, he soon gained renown for his scholarship, and attained high rank among his kind despite his radical anti-war beliefs.
Accipiter says: And one day, this enterprising hawk embarked upon a certain project...he flew to an island south of Wayhaven;a desolate though fertile isle, and spent the greater part of the next forty years planting a magical forest ripe with all species of trees.
Accipiter says: When my creation was complete, I offered it to the man/trees as a gesture of peace, as a message that at least one man/bird remains averse to the violence of years past.
Accipiter says: And yea, once our Power gained word of my offering, I found myself here, on the cold ground, remanded to a fate of flightless impotency. A bittersweet tale, yea

You say: hi
Cocodryllus says: Truly I am in no mood for pedestrian chat, adventurer. Begone, yea

You say: moon tree
Cocodryllus's right eye flashes.Cocodryllus says: It be the Moon Tree ye seek? True, ye be close, as it lie just beyond this creek. But to visit our fair Mother, I'm afraid, is quite out of the question. You see, since with only one eye I cannot tell friend from foe, alas you may not pass.

You say: eye
Cocodryllus growls: My eye was snatched by the wicked serpent, Anguis.
You say: anguis
Cocodryllus says: Ah, we have a long history of enmity, he and I. He is but a wee snake, ye see...but he caught me unawares last night, and plucked my eye from my brainpan.
Cocodryllus says: He slithered off before I could lay chase. He is probably back in his rocky refuge by now.
Cocodryllus says: I wonder how he even made it to this isle. Perhaps he stowed away in some adventurer's boat.
You say: rocky
You say: refuge
Cocodryllus snarls: The piteous beast finds home in brief rock settlements, and prefers unbearably hot, dry conditions. Indeed, he is not a native of this island.

Charter forest of types at the ferry.

43) Heart of the Cosmos: Find the USA today that is floating around chaos/study horoscope. Go to each of the 12 houses and kill all of the mobs. 55) Shadowrun: First: map Atlanta (in science) otherwise you'll get lost.

Find Mr Johnson in Atlanta. He is located 2w, 2n, 2w from the subway entrance.

Speak to him about the quest, then follow these steps:

1. First, get the door remover in the gunshop on the south end of Avery Street by killing the guy in the 2nd room. (subway, 1w, 9s, 2w).

2. Activate the remover in the activator 5n and 4e, d from the subway entrance.

3. Go to the green lightning gang hideout (1w, 7s, 3e, s) and remove the door that is 2 south and up from the entrance. Kill the leader for the passcard. He is 47k, but only has one attack.

4. Activate the passcard in the activator in the north east corner of town. From the subway, 4n, 6e, 2n, e, s.

5. The go down to the parking garage (2e, n from subway) and go down to the 5th sublevel. In the northwest corner of the 5th level insert passcard.

6. Enter and kill the drone. It will die easily. Go past it and get the datachip. Then get out of the garage. 

7. Go and activate the datachip in the 3rd activator, which you have not used yet. It is located 7e from the subway. Then go and give the activated datachip to Mr. Johnson in the bar in the northwest part of town.

8. He will give you 10k coins and the qps.. (30)

65) Miyu: This is the only one I'm providing a map for. Look for a boy wandering around chaos. look at him, type: trace symbol, and you're in the Miyu area.

The directions to this area take a while to get used to: they aren't n, s, e, w. Instead it uses left, right, forwards, backwards, and the orientation depends totally from what direction you entered the room from. You'll get used to it. Go to H on the map. Search houses, enter house. Once inside house, search debris. You'll find a mirror, which the boy in the house will take. Kill boy, get mirror. Also look at the picture on the wall here. Go out, and go to L on the map. Search the records, and you find a diary. Kill the boy here (he takes the diary before you can).Read the diary.. it gives some history to the quest. Go to T.. this is where the vampire Miyu is. Go back one space from her. Drop all your gear. Then go back into the temple. Say hi, and she asks if she can bite you. Say yes, then type: bite me. She bites you, and reduces you to 1 hp. When she bites you, she also makes you drop everything you were carrying, and she takes it. This is why you drop your stuff in the other room. Heal yourself. get your gear, and then go to the Armor (marked A on map). Look at the mirror. Use mirror. Type: use mirror on armor. Then kill the armor. This armor is tough... but you can't kill it at all unless you use the mirror on it first, and have been bitten by Miyu. When Armor is dead, sever head from corpse. get head. Go back to H, enter house, place head in picture. (40)

73) Ring of Power: Go to the zoo in chaos. From Da Void, it's n, w, n, and then search around a bit.. it's near the hide and seek quest. Enter the zoo, go 3n into zookeeper's house. Move the rug and get the key to open the drawer in his desk. Get the journal and read it all. Go s, 4w, s, sw, w, kill polar bear, get feather. Go e, ne, 4n, enter tree, kill lion, get horn. Leave the tree, go 2s, nw, w, kill panther, get tail. Go e, se, s, enter house, kill zookeepers. Clean mirror, gaze mirror. You are transported to place with a maze. Now, make sure you have plenty of healing... lots of maze guardians that don't hit hard, but there can be lots of them. Also make sure you have something to mark your way through the maze or you will be terminally lost! Enter the maze. You will soon find that directions don't correspond: so that if you go left to get to one room, if you then go right you probably won't end up back where you began. So mark the rooms and work out the directions. There are 15 rooms total. When I did it, the directions to the end were: forward, forward, left, left, backwards, left, left, backwards, left, left, forward, right, forward, and you should be at castle. Don't enter the castle yet! Search stone, go down, kill dragon (68k). Put horn in conical hole, put feather in oblong hole, put tail in cylindrical hole, get ring of power. Then go up. If you need healing go back, else enter castle, go up, kill wizard (he's fairly nasty, but not TOO bad, 71k), enter crack, melt ring in lava. (55)

74) The Project: Enter Science, u/4n/d/2n/11w/nw. Go a couple north and west until you see a compound (it's a small area, so it won't take you long to find it). Enter the compound and then go all the way north to the shuttle to Mars. There is a messenger here that you can speak to. Ask him about Mars and mines and stuff. Go to the shuttle, enter it and go to Mars. On Mars you're inside a large covered colony. Map it. The shuttle is in the most north eastern part of the colony. The areas aren't really very big, so it won't take you long to map it. From the shuttle, go:2 sw, w, sw, w, d, 2w, sw, nw, n, nw, n, ne, n, enter massage parlor. You can speak to the woman at the back by the stairs. Go up the stairs and into a room with a woman in it. If she has a passcard then kill her and get it. If she doesn't then you'll need to look around on wandering workers for one (correct ID Badge will have a small security symbol on it, I found it upstairs in the bar in the north of the plaza, think it was search bed, but moves around). Leave the massage parlor, go back s, sw, s, se, s, se, then go: sw, 2s, and into the large plaza area. Wander around here until you find a tourist with a camcorder. Kill them and get it. You'll need the camcorder to record what you see down in the mines. In the north east part of this plaza is the news office, where you'll need to take the info you get to solve the quest. Find the secret genetics lab. From where you entered on the shuttle, go: 2sw, w, nw, n, w, and use the elevator to go down. Wander about in the mines until you find a door with a card reader. You'll need to use the passcard that you got to open the door and enter the lab. If you can't find the door in these mines, then try the mines on the surface of the planet. First buy an environment suit from the shop in the south east area of the plaza. If you leave the colony without it then you'll die. Wear the suit! Then go to the airlock in the sw area of the plaza, and go out on to the surface of the planet. From here, go: 5w, 2n, e (hidden exit)and into the mines here. Once you enter the lab, immediately attack the scientist here(Dr. Gnolwright - he is no leave, 50k)). Kill him. He'll summon orderlies to attack you, so if you have some sort of calming power then use it. Once he's dead, then go east into his office. Search through the computer stuff. Search disks until you find one that looks important. Get disk. Then go back west, n to a pit. Look at the pit full of bodies. Start recording on the camcorder (the description tells you how). Stop recording again. Then go back to the news woman in the plaza in the colony. She'll immediately take the objects that you have. (55)

76) Megatech: The new Megatech is a lot harder then the old one. You have to go from the subway, u,4w,3s,all w, kill enforcers, n, 2w, n, kill enforcers open door, west, free man, and talk to him. In each room you have to 'search', and in some you find a panel. One should say just that it's black, but the one you want to find is the one that is long, and it has '[ready]' on it. Now when you find the [ready], insert the lowest number of the passkeys you have (should get a 3,5,7,10) and so on. On level 300, use passkey 3, and on level 350 use passkey 5 and such, this is the hard part. Anyway, once inside, the directions are approximately: for level 50->100, all east, all s, should be like 3 or 5n, then go west. 'search' in each room for them and you'll find panels in some. Look at panel and when you see a [ready] insert the correct passkey (lowest one that you have) check the numbers by look at front of passkey. On floor 500 go all west to Ancient Western dragon and kill it. Go west again and kill Arnold Hesler. (65)

82) Perplexus: OK, as the quest description says, go to Angelo, and look for the angel. From the west gate of Wayhaven (which is 12 west of the Wayhaven portal) go: 7n,14w,2s,bow (to Led), s, and you're in Angelo. Kill the guards on the main road here, and get the key. Go west, and into the guard outpost. Kill the guards, search around, there's a trapdoor under the table. Move the table. unlock trapdoor, open, go down... follow the tunnels, killing cockroaches as you go. Where the tunnel forks, ignore the route to the troll, and go the other way (east). A few east, where the tunnel ends, you have to enter something or do something like that, and you'll find the angel. Speak to her.. use keywords like 'hello', 'help', 'Perplexus'...and anything else that comes up. She'll tell you that to find out more, you have to speak to the old wise elf. And she'll tell you that he lives in the mountains to the north. If she still has it, she will give you a holy avenger sword (useful for killing the evil elf king later). Leave the tunnels, and back out onto the main road, while you're in town, have a look around: a couple south and one east of where you are, there's a statue of Perplexus... this is really Perplexus who has been turned to stone. Go back west, and a couple south along the main road, until you can't go any further. There's a strange wall to the west. 'push wall' and you'll end up behind it. Go 3 west, 2s and enter the tower, or castle, or whatever. Go 2 east, 3s, kill the 3 guards. Go 3 up, north, kill Goliath. Search painting, and you'll find a back room. There's Armor of the Dragon here (unbreakable, +3 strength), and 'quillions' which is part of the sword of Perplexus. Make sure you get this item! Go: out, s, 3d, 3n, 3w (back to tower entry). This time, go 2 west, 3s,m kill guards, 3u, n, kill Kargile. (this guy is a bit tougher than Goliath). Move plaque, and you'll enter a back room, this time you'll find the amulet of Perplexus.. keep this! To get back to town, go: out, 3d,3n,2e, leave,2n,4east. Head about 6 north (until you can't go any further), and you'll be out of town. From here, you need to get to the northern mountains. The direct route, I think, is:7e,6n. Or, from the west gate of Wayhaven, it's: 3 west,12 north, 4west, north. Once you get to there, 'climb' twice. Go s, w, n, w, n, kill lich. The lich should have the handle for the sword. Keep the handle! Go s,e,directly south for a few...somewhere here you go 2d, kill golem, go n to cave kill Mamakin. 'enter gap' get the blade, and you have the 3 components for the sword! DON'T make the sword yet!!!! As if you have to drop it or give it to someone, it vanishes, and the quest is ruined. Go out, s,2u,n, go east as far as you can, until you find a tree... climb rope., e, u, and speak to Elistan, who will tell you more info about where the wise elf is. If you're not carrying the holy avenger sword, that the angel had, then he won't tell you much, but that's OK. Go 2e,2d. There's a bedroom to the south. Look at the dresser.. there are 5 drawers. Search all the drawers (search drawer1, search drawer 2 etc.). You should find a diary (read this.. gives you more info) and a key. Go north out of the bedroom again. There's a door in the floor: open door and go down. Go west and speak to the queen (don't remember her name) she'll tell you a little more about where the wise elf lives, and also tell you to ignore any messages saying he's not in. Go west, n,d, out,w,4s,about 15 east, till there's a house to the north. Go north. There's a sign saying that the wise one's out... ignore this and unlock gate (with the key from the dresser) enter the house. kill the guards, go north to an empty room. search fireplace, move brick, get crystal. Touch crystal (must be in this room), and the wise elf (Yeltor) will appear. He'll tell you what to do for the quest, if you talk to him. He tells you to go see the scout in the village. Leave by going south a few times, and you'll end up back at the main path. Go back about 2 west, till there's a road to the south. Go south, east, ring bell, and the scout will come. say help, say quest, and he'll ask you who sent you... say 'Yeltor' Then he'll ask you to show him an item of Perplexus... show him the amulet. He'll tell you to nod when you're ready. Now this is the good bit: only one person is supposed to be able to get into the gray elves tree at a time... but once he's been shown the amulet, anybody can 'nod' and be allowed entry. So you can take a tank with you, to fight the creatures you have to fight. nod, and you'll be escorted into the back room. Go d, 2e,ne,4e,u,e (kill, or ignore the gray elves along the way). You're at the entry to the gray elves' tree. As mentioned in Elistan's diary, there's some twigs by the door. (look at the panels to the left and right of the door). Now, if you get the combo wrong, then you may be roped up by your feet, and you need a knife of some sort from one of the monsters in the area to cut the rope, otherwise the only way out is to quit. If this happens, you lose everything. So: before you try the combo, drop all your gear! Especially the quest items. If you get strung up then you can quit but you have to come back and start over again. If the door opens, and you don't get roped up, then get all your gear, and enter the tree. Go east, to a major intersection of tunnels. Now according to Elistan's diary, you have to put something in a large bowl, to open another door. From the intersection, go se, and follow it south. Search rags and you'll find an elf. talk to him a bit using key words. he'll reveal that if you place a stone in a bowl to the south, then you can take a rock from a room to the north, and drop it (he doesn't say where to drop it). Go back to the major intersection of tunnels. This time go ne, east for a few. There's a set of tunnels forking off: ne,e,se In each of these rooms is a priest. In each case, kill the priest, search the altar, and get the precious stone. You should have a ruby, and emerald, and a sapphire. Go back west, sw, to the major intersection. There is possibly a trap to the south, so drop your gear here. Just take the ruby with you. This time take the south corridor... look at markings on the wall. They will show what gem has to go in what bowl. Go north.. if you have done the bowl bit wrong, you'll fall into a pit and have to quit. Go north.. collect your gear. Go about 3 north, to the end of the corridor. Kill the skull. Go west: a room on some sort of springs... interesting, but you don't know what to do... Go back 2 east, a room with a rock in it. Now that the ruby's in the bowl, and you have both other gems in your hands... you should be able to lift the rock. Go back to west to the springy room. Make sure both you and your tank are in the room. drop the roc and! the spring floor will drop, and deposit you in another room. Go west, kill the priests. Look at fountain. look at skull. Swivel skull. A secret door opens to the south. Go south, and kill the gray elf king. Make sure you have a tank! Get the cloak of Perplexus! Go back north.. l at altar, search altar. press switch until a portal opens up. Enter it, and you're back on the trail in the forest, north east of where the scout is. Go back west as far as you can, then go back east one. Go 4 north, east, in, u,s,2u,2w,d,w,d,2w,n,2d (out of the mountains) Go back to Angelo: from here, it should be: 6s,7w,2s,bow,3s,e. here, or around here, is the statue of Perplexus... Holding the 3 pieces of the sword: handle, blade, and quillions, type: make sword, and the ego sword is made. type: place sword. type: place cloak type: place amulet and, the statue will come to life. (75)

83) Pyron: (75)

84) Dragon Knight: Go to the Portal of Life. From forest portal it's: 3w, 2sw, 2s, 2e.Good luck trying to map it. The area is dotted with following wyverns, which aren't hard to kill. Object: free the queen from being entombed in stone. To do this you need 5 colored orbs that you get from killing the dragon knights, and the Staff of the Positive Plane to kill the High Cleric who guards her. You also need a hexagonal key and an octagonal key to get to her. OK, go to green keep, kill guards (easy), n, e, search hearth, get rusty key,w, n, ne, 2u, n, push stone (on pillar), get red key. Ignore all other items here. Go to blue keep, kill guards, n, w, search hearth, unlock door (with rusty key), hearth, search look at brick, l at symbols, push stone/button, get green key. Go back to green keep, 2n, nw, 2u, unlock door with green key, n, there is a dragon knight here. Wait for a minute and he will turn into a green dragon and attack. Kill him (he's not too hard). Get the green orb. Never wimpy from a dragon knight or demons come and attack you, and they are annoying. Go to the 'wiz tree'. There is something in the description about an odd tree here. Search, turn knob, enter, u, and you will see an elven wizard. Say help, and he will give you a rainbow amulet. Wear this. Go to red stronghold. kill guards, 2n, ne, 2u, n, make sure you're wearing the rainbow amulet, and enter. Make sure nobody follows you in. There is a pillar here. Push stone, get blue key. Leave the room and go down, sw. This time go nw, 2u, unlock door with red key, n, wait till dragon knight turns into dragon, kill him, get red orb. Go to blue keep again, 2n, nw, 2u, unlock door with blue key, n, and there is a bench here. Lay on bench, dragon knight comes, kill blue dragon, get blue orb. Go to village. Follow the path into the center of the village, and then the wise woman is off to the nw. Go to her, and say help. She will give you a torch. Leave the village and go to white keep. Kill guards, 2n and you see a fountain. Melt ice (need that torch). Get scroll. Go ne, 2u, n, push stone (on pillar) and get black key. Go to black keep. Kill guards, 2n, nw, 2u, unlock door with black key, n, kill black dragon knight, get black orb. Go s, 2d, ne, 2u, n, kill cleric. Push stone (on pillar). get white key. If you enter the doorway here you will go straight back to white keep. Go to white keep, 2n, nw, 2u, unlock door with white key, n, kill dragon knight, and get white orb. OK, now you should have all the dragon orbs! You need the more keys and the staff: Go to wyvern nest, climb (up into nest). Kill all 4 wyverns, search nest and you should find the staff of the positive plane. If not, go searching around the cliffs for more nests. You can insert one of the orbs into the staff, but don't try this right now, because you'll lose the orb and will have to go get another. Go to lizard nest. Climb up, kill faerie lizards, search nest and you should find a crystal key. If not search around for more nests.

Hexagonal Key: Go to place marked Temple on map, search bushes, enter, look at murals, move brick, get hexagonal key.

Octagonal Key: The octagonal key is on a courier who wanders in the area. I have always found him in the north east section. Follow him and kill him (easy). Get octagonal key. 

When you're ready for the final assault on the palace, look at the scroll. Chant the words on the scroll and you end up at the cliff where you have to 'search cliff' and go up. Actually, this place is 7n of the portal of life, and you don't need the scroll at all to get there. Go up, n, kill lich, 2 or 3n, till you see a pillar. Unlock pillar (with crystal key) and the drawbridge comes down. Go north and into palace. The palace is basically a square, with a tower at each corner. In each tower is a device you need to unlock (using hex or octagonal key). When this happens the pyramid they were supporting floats to the ground and you can go in to free the queen.

What you do is: from just inside palace, go: w, kill cleric (no wimpy, but he's not too hard), sw, up, kill lich, (no wimpy), u, unlock device. 2d, ne, 2e, kill cleric (no wimpy), se, up, now there is a lich here who won't let you go up. Kill him, and you can go 2u, unlock device, 2d, kill lich, nw, 2n, kill cleric (no wimpy), ne, u, dispose of the lich, u, unlock device, 2d, sw, 2w (past a couple of clerics, but they allow you to wimpy), nw, u, dispose of lich, u, unlock device. Now all the devices are inactivated, and the pyramid should come down. Go 2d, se, e, kill the 2 clerics, 2s, wield the staff of the positive plane, kill cleric. He should vaporize with the first hit. Get out all 5 orbs, look at the stone, and insert orbs. When you do this, the queen is freed, and the quest is done! 

Notes: If you let the lich follow you any further than the base of the tower, then it will stop you leaving and you will have to fight it to the death. The liches take a while to kill, so they are annoying. If you have somebody as a tank in the palace, don't wield the staff of the positive plane until you have to kill the final cleric. If you are wielding the staff then monsters will attack you, even if someone is trying to defend. (80)

88) Balooga Falls: Note: You'll need an anchor. Go to the bridge and knock out the pegs, then grab or hold rope before you knock them out. Go to nyrow. say hi, quest, demons, jobs, angeldemons. 4w/n/e/n/look at painting/look at bench/open bench/get map/look at map. The go s/say hi/say angeldemons/say falls/say barrel/w/s/3w/look at monument. look at base, look at hole (search just to play dumb 3s/5e, say {hi, job, quest, demons, god, false god, gnos, monument} 4w/2n/5w, pray to gnos or just pray. Kill Lars treetop, get all. n/3e/4n/wade into water or wade into river. climb into barrel (you'll get that from Lars). Here is the "quest" part. (look at everything just to play dumb) n/3e, walk between poles. n kill demon (not so hard, 20K I think) Break mirror, n/get all/3s/ walk between poles/4w/nw/3n. kill all guards (EASY) get all/w/n/se/arch and finally search liquid (You get 1 gem). s/e/s unlock door, open door w, free prisoner, open door e/2s/2se/2e/n. kill Caveman and go 2n/climb idol. climb idol and pry left eye (I think it was if not do the other, you take some damage if you pry the wrong one- this is gem 2). Go n/w , say gnos and you'll get hit by water, so you lose ALL HP except one, you don't die, turn off all "panic buttons" before you do this. Turn your "panic buttons" back on and go e/n/step into light. Go n/w kill all, hole, kill all get all, out/2e, jump across (DONT JUMP FOR ROPE, look at it and search it but DONT JUMP FOR IT, you'll get thrown out of the game if you do) climb down, search, get all (gem 3), climb east wall. n door, say 200 (its a riddle you get thrown out of the game if you get the wrong answer), notice the name he says... like "Say hi to blah for me", and notice his name.) 2n/w, get parchment, look at parchment.. (You should do this before anything else) and then afterwards go get the mirror gem and such. search throne, search hand, arm, search left arm rest (and right arm rest) open one of them (I think it was the right), and get gem (4). Go e/2n/ne/e look at skull, look at balls. throw balls at skull. You now get gem 5. Go w/n/nw/w/avert eyes from cage, pull rope, kill gorgon get amm (gem 6) e/n. Say hi, gems demons, gnos, angeldemons. You should go to this guy first too, (after stilts and parchment because he gives you lots of good information, about the room of the kings (throne room). Ok.... Right n is a DEATHTRAP... To avoid it, you should type pray to gnos every round.. He will save you.. BUT if you are lagging... R.I.P. My advice is to trigger this to go every round. Search/get all (gem7)/n/say hi, he will say "I don't talk to strangers". Remember the name at the riddle dude, say Byro n.. He will ask who told you, say Ragorse. Then to let him pass, say false god or quest or something. Right n is a VERY DANGEROUS Hydra, class 120K or something. You have to kill him, but there is a trick that might just work. Try to go north and back s to the manticore, and then n again, hopefully he will let you pass. If not you have to kill him. Go n until you come to a door, search it and search holes. Here is the right sequence you should put the gems in. If not it's been changed: Hole 7=Emerald. Hole 6=Ruby. Hole 5=Sapphire. Hole 4=Diamond. Hole 3=Pearl. Hole 2=Opal. Hole 1=Topaz. Go all n and look at painting. look at EVERY item on the painting. Then finally look at moon. Step through the wall (it will say the correct syntax for you) and get all and say GO you will get transported out to Balooga falls. Find your way to nyrow, (think it's just go n). Then go 6w/3s/6e (You'll be back at the priest). say staff, anchor, and the third item you got. He will say The staff get it's energy from hearts of demons. look at staff. You will notice its base is "screwed" (the hole in the monument is also screwed). So kill ALL 21 demons, carry ALL hearts in your inventory, and go to the monument and type insert staff in monument (or hole). Kill false god. The god hunts so be careful not to drag him to town and let some other asshole kill him. (90)

89) Wayhaven: First: map all of Wayhaven. 
From the portal go: 5e/5s/e and climb stairs to the clerk. 
Present yourself and he'll tell you that you need citizenship.
Enter the stall n/w of portal and buy a guitar. 
Then go to the woman on balcony (6n/2e of portal). 
Serenade woman and receive her message. 
Find the captain of the guard (4s/climb staircase from portal) and deliver message.
He'll give you another message. 
Go back to the woman and deliver the new message. 
She gives you a note, take this to the guild master 
(e/2n/w/enter door/w/present note from woman). 
He gives you guild sponsorship. 
Go back to the clerk and present yourself. 
He tells you to get a bounty hunter's license. 
Go to tintorillos (w/s of clerk) and 'prepare document'.
They'll tell you that you need ink and notarized paper. 
Go to the ink shop (n/w/5n/7e/2n/2e/3n/4w/2n/e from tintorillos). 
Ink master tells you that you need an ink fish 
(w/n/4w/s/kill fisherogre/get rod/catch fish). 
Go back to ink master and buy ink. 
Go to the paper shop (w/n/3w/4n from ink shop) and buy legal bond paper.
Go get it notarized (3w/2 or 3s from clerk). 
There's a sign saying that the notary office is along the Promenade.
You can't get there unless you have a pass so go to the printer shop
(12e/2n/2e/2n/w from portal) and buy pass. 
He'll tell you to go to a forger and 'shimmy on out of here'. 
Shimmy and you'll go up a ladder to the forger. 
He needs special and ink and paper so guess where you get to go again! 
Come back and get your pass. Go back to the Promenade 
(5e/5s/w/3s/3e from portal) and 'notarize document'. 
Go e/n search the dock. Leap to the boat you find, 
free smuggler and he'll take you back and give you an important item.
Go back to tintorillos (see why you need to map Wayhaven??) 
and 'prepare document' by going s of the clerk and typing 'sign document'.
The 5 councilors each need a bribe, and each bribe is different. 
1: a gem (dwarven traders north of portal), 
2) a gladhand (hustler in se section of Wayhaven), 
3) a book on making money 
(Wayhaven library: 7w/3s/2e/2s/u/w from portal. 
Kill everyone, search the shelves and steal book), 
4) a drow tapestry (go to gunpowder shop [s/3e/n of paper shop] and buy gunpowder.
Go to the citadel cannon [4s/2w/3s of portal], light cannon, and climb in cannon.
Go through the citadel and kill the guards. 
Kill the captain and step in haze. 
Kill the guards, climb up, kill more guards, and go west. 
Kill the guards, but not the sergeants. 
Keep heading west, kill the captain, and go west and then north. 
Search a few rooms north and get the tapestry. Give it to the councilor), 
5: silver dragon scale (challenge arena [4n/e/d from portal] 
and challenge the baby silver dragon. 
Kill it and get the scale.) 
Once you have all 5 signatures go back to the clerk and present yourself.
He tells you about the quest. 
Head to the brothel (8e/3s/3e/2n/e from portal). 
Peruse the book and request a whore. 
You need to go the guild HQ (8n/5e/2n/e from portal) and request guild membership.
Buy thread and velvet from the stalls in the bazaar (s/w and s/e from portal) 
and go to the seamstress (12e/2n/2e/7n from portal) where you order a sash. 
Go back to the brothel, order a whore, and pleasure him/her. 
Request the madam and kill her. She escapes through a secret door. 
Search around, go through the secret door, kill her, get the papers and the key. 
Search around to find the exit again. 
Now, go to the chief mugger in the mews (5e/4n/e/3s/e from portal) 
and kill the mugger (who has a dwarf mask). 
Go w/3n/4w/s/e/s and wear the mask to go into the dwarven pub. 
Kill the 5 dwarves that attack you and search the mirror and go down 
through the trap door. Then go n/e and search around. 
Open the door you find with the key you got from the madam. 
Kill the chief mugger who attacks (80k) and then search around to get his seal. 
You also find a secret exit leading you out to a safe place. 
Go back to the clerk and present yourself again. 
As you head to the mayor's office you fall into a well. 
Blow the whistle you got from the smuggler and he'll come and take you to a 
secret entrance. Search the ladder (to disarm a trap). 
Climb up and kill the mayor. (95)

73) Vole the Hateful: REMOVED 

Go to Deep Mountain and find the drow translator. Go to level 4 of the underdark maze and get the maul of the titans. Go to the 'open fields' and 'dig' 20 or 30 times in each room until you hear a rumbling sound. It will say you fell into a hole or something, dig until it says you can't anymore. Listen to what you're told and you'll be given a strand of beads. Hang on to this! Go back to level 4 of the maze and listen at the dusty corner until you hear someone mumble something. Make a note of what word is mumbled. Go to the demon spider and kill it. Search the throne and open door, go down and search around. You'll be asked for a password (this is the word you heard mumbled). Keep going and head south at the first intersection you run into. Break beads and watch the show. Note: be VERY careful of the demon spider. If you're lucky you'll get the demon spider carapace from it (a nice piece of armor). (80)

16.  ( Complete ) [* 10*]  Disney                Not solved this 
reboot.
Go to the west until you can go south.  Then go all south and all west 
until you find Doc at the mine.  Say diamond and he'll give you a 
pickaxe.
  Swing pickaxe in every room of the mine until you find the diamond, 
then go back to where you went south.  Head all west to the house in 
the forest and go in.  Give the diamond to Snow White and say mirror.  
She'll give you a mirror.  Go all e from the beginning until you can 
swim, swim, go first s, kill ursula, s, get letter, go back to witch, 
show letter to witch, talk to witch until she says she wants the 
mirror, 
show mirror to witch, give mirror to witch.plan  She drops the award, 
pick it up and go back to the mirror.  Head south and check out the 
first house to the west.  Inside is Mickey, give the award to him.


17.  ( Not Done ) [  10 ]  Djinni                Not solved this 
reboot.
Djinni: Djinni Bring a light source.
Wayhaven, all e, leave, folow road e/ne until you get to the docks.  
In the room before either dock (exits e or n) swim or swim in ocean.
  Swim until you get to another beach with only exit south.  
Go s and then climb over rocks then examine cliff, examine 
cave etc.  Dive water, watch mob until it settles on the bottom, 
kill mob, examine bottom, search slime, get bottle.  
(Key you get from mob can be used to open a tan box on 
the island in this area to get a tan marble).

Once you 
have the bottle, return home or to a good area.  
You may want to put eq in a box as you can't use 
eq or guild powers once inside the bottle.
Remove cork.

You now suck.  I will only say the 
things you have to do - you may want to kill the
 mobs to get eq as you will have none.
Go to the room with Stinky/Skippy/whatever his name is
 - he is the newbie.  
Here you can pick flowers for a 100 hp heal.  
Left of him is a room with an anorexic slave.  
You can exa garden, pick vegetables, get vegetables.
Each vegetable gives approx 100 hp heal.  You will need these!
Go to the mage, wait until he says the magic word 'Kazam'  
To the right of the mage, search rocks for a hunting knife, 
this helps ALOT!  Go to centre and say key in front of a mob 
(I did this with the rogue but I assume it will work for any of them).
Mob will tell you which little mob in the outer circle has their 
particular key.
Go to them and say key again.  
They will give you a key to the door.
Kill guard in inner circle (I found him pretty hard), 
unlock door, go 2n - here is the mage (non-aggro)  
I would suggest having as many flowers/vegetables and ppl available 
for hmheal from afar as possible for this bit.
Kill mage, get sword. Go s, search room, say kazam, 
climb stairs, give sword to Djinni. (10)

Portentous Shoppe                                                 
---*---  
                                                                   / | 
\ 
                                                                           

The overwhelming exhibit of dramatic objects d'art creates an
oppressive atmosphere.  The small space is sheathed in a gloominess
that is formed from the dark decor, not the lack of adequate lighting.
In a final insult to the senses, suffocating the fresh air is the
mingled odour of dust, incense and the musty smell of aged paper.
    There are two obvious exits: exit, north                             
Cuthbert Pottly.
> list

exa staff
A branch of wood as white as purest ivory, this short staff is 
decorated and
inscribed with designs formed by orange sand and turquoise jelly.  The 
origin
of these strange and serpentine images is truly not of the present

exa designs
The images on the staff appear to be totally disordered at first.  As
you gaze closer, you begin to see patterns emerge from the chaos. 
Suddenly, as if your mind and eyes are focusing in unison for the first
time, the majesty of the overall design becomes clear.  You are
awestricken by the power bound up in this staff and fear what might
happen if the pattern was traced and the power unleashed.               
trace pattern
As you trace the pattern on the staff, bright sparks of
white light dance around in your wake.  Surges of energy
course through your body; almost more than you can bear!
You almost give up in agony, when suddenly, you finish.
The staff is definitely warmer, but there doesn't seem to
have been any apocalyptic, or even interesting, results.
You look around, half in disappointment, half in anticipation.
The quarterstaff warms to your grasp.
The quarterstaff warms to your grasp.
The staff abruptly turns cold!
The hoary, freezing sensation becomes almost unbearable --
it feels more blistering than the breath of a red dragon,
yet you are unable to loosen your grip!
The artifact suddenly bursts into flame, an icy white 
conflagration which envelops your hand, and soon your
entire arm!
The silver blaze consumes your shoulder, your torso...unable
even to think, you watch with awe and dread as your entire body
is soon indistinguishable from the flame itself!
A deafening clap of energy resounds forth from within your body!
Another burst of searing sound, as though a barrier were
being razed!  
Three more blasts of deafening proportions, in quick succession!
You can see nothing around you except a light beyond that of the sun!
...then, silence...the deepest depths of silence, a state
beyond peace...
...at the center of your vision, barely outlined by a soft aura of
white light, you see a shape...you cannot discern whether the
image exists in space before you, or in your very mind...
As you gaze at the figure, you find yourself thinking the 
following words:
'I must move to the center of my world...'
'...once there, I must look up, towards the sky...'
'...at that time, I will begin to understand.'
The image fades, and as the light surrounding it dies down,
you sense that the moment has ended...
The artifact, once burned into your hand, has disappeared.
Sight returns to your eyes, darkness becomes light again.
COT
look up
You turn your gaze skyward, and fix your eyes upon the world above...
...the multicolored sky appears as it always does, but gradually...
...shapes in the sky begin to become apparent to you...the pompous
clouds gently round their edges and project sinews of mist in the
vague suggestion of...faces!
...and these faces, these half-realities that seem to exist partly
in your very mind, begin to assume the countenances of men...
...shifting your gaze about, you notice that the entire sky, the
limitless expanse a horizon around, is alive with these faces,
expressions of the very essence of peace...
...a slim, blue face floats in front of a wide, indigo face, both
smiling upon you as though you were an honored visitor to their
reality......seemingly swimming in the molasses of the infinite space, 
these 
benevolent profiles collectively close their eyes towards you,
and you feel a slight shiver budding from inside your heart...
...you glance down in a momentary response towards the subtle
pain in your chest -- it is both a pain of envy and of bliss...
...as you quickly raise your eyes back up to the skies, still
cowering slightly over your heart, you see that the faces have
gone, slipped back into the hilts and scabbards of the clouds 
and constellations...
...you are left with the vague knowledge that there exists a
dimension of life far above this one, where thoughts pass as
though silent lightning through the clouds, and where a bliss
may be found amongst the brash spirits of the wind and rain.

town.

in the northwest part of town.
