Qinfo (last updated 12/12/98)
The majority of these are written from memory so the exact syntax might 
not be included.  While there are directions for some of the quests, 
THERE ARE NO MAPS.  Those of us who did the quests on our own had to map 
and explore...SO SHALL YOU.  This is good for you because if you go 
through like a laundry list you WILL get popped for qinfo.  Numbers that 
aren't listed have been removed from the game.  Special thanks to all 
the people who helped by providing information on quests I haven't done.  
No names (for security reasons), but you know who you are.  Whenever 
possible I've added notes about possible death traps and toughness of 
mobs.  

1) Marbles: these are found all over the mud. See Marble List. (1qp 
each)
2) Tree: from cot: s/2e/2s/look at tree. (5)
4) Resource Crisis: newbie land, find the mirror with the oil field in 
it. Search behind the seat of the truck. In the tool shed, in the 
office desk and just everywhere. You need a digital multimeter and a pair of 
wire clippers. Then, after you have those, find the tower you can climb 
up. There's a device. Test each wire with the multimeter.  The one with 
the charge is the one you need to clip. (5)
5) Newbie Academy: from newbie bin, go s, d, n and enroll in the 
school.  Answer all the questions, they answers are all in help files and 
room descriptions.  Make sure you know the phone number to the White 
House. If you aren't a newbie, you can still do this quest. In the sewers of 
Pinnacle look for the newbie mice and you're on your way. (5)
6) Mack: find the duploland mirror in newbie land.  Find the bone 
somewhere in there.  You'll have to search around.  Give it to the dog, 
he'll give you a piece of a key.  Buy a donut and give it to the duplocop.  
Go into the jail cell and find the password (C1FB as far as I know).  
Take it to the bank and ask the teller for the box.  In it is the other 
half of the key.  Find the stepladder and go to the house and find the 
trapdoor leading up.  Go up, n, unlock door, open door, w and kill 
Mack. (5)
7) Free Cho: chaos/enter/4w/e/s/e. you need to activate the machine by 
pulling levers flipping switches, pushing buttons, etc.  Kill all the 
mobs you see in there.  Careful, as this is no wimpy.  After you kill 
all of them, eventually you'll see Dr. Cho. Type 'free Cho' and finish 
killing the mobs. Then you're done! (5)
8) Codename Kodiak: in newbie land, find the battletech mirror and go 
in. go nw/nw/e/nw/nw/nw and go into the elevator shaft. Go up and talk 
to the guy. Then, go back down into the elevator, and then search the 
boards. Go down and talk to the guy there, he'll give you a helmet. Wear 
the helmet and go u/se/se/se/w/se/sw/se/sw/and search trees. You'll see 
a hidden exit ONLY if you wear the helmet. Go kill Kodiak. (5)
9) Chop Tree: you need an axe and some patience for this one.  Search 
all the rooms in each of the mirrors with your trusty axe.  You'll find 
an old oak tree.  When you find it, just type 'chop tree' and you're 
done. (5)
10) Bug: No qinfo for this one.  The mosquito flies around pinnacle and 
everyone is free to attack it.  It can take massive amounts of damage, 
so dedicate some time for this.  It will randomly leave to another 
place in Pinnacle, and might just port you somewhere else randomly.  Only 
problem I can find is getting it after it's gone into the cemetery. (5)
11) Bbn Planet: chaos/2w/lift manhole cover/n/kill tech (5k)/search 
wall/kill tech (5k)/plug DCR.NET cable into lower server (5)
12) Zetron: Fantasy/city portal.  Go 2n/w/enter stall and buy a medium 
sized ladder.  Go 3 or 4 east from that stall and enter the next one 
and buy incense.  Go to the portal and search portal, retrieve seal. Then 
go 7w/6s/3w/s and find the shrine to Zetron. Burn incense, pray, return 
seal. (10)
14) Spaceport: chaos/enter/2n/w/u/board shuttle/pull lever like 4 
times.  Go to the desert and find the fremen. Kill them and get the comb.  
Comb desert.  Go n from there and blow up the death star and kill the 
emperor.  Get his heart. Then find the statue and search the statue. Go 
inside the little gift shop thing and buy an amulet/medallion. Go back 
out to the statue and practice on it. Or raise statue. I don't recall, 
but toy around with it. Then go s to where there's a creature. Kill 
Vader and get HIS heart. Go back to yoda and give the 2 hearts to yoda. 
(10)
15) Save Grandma: chaos/all s/ne. You'll be in a forest. Search every 
room for a red cloak. Wear the cloak and go to the house in the 
northeast corner. Knock on door. Kill the wolf and open closet. (10)
16) Sarkath Khan: fantasy/city portal/12n/leave/8n/5w/2n/path/enter. 
Order room/order beer/sit/give beer to zarkoff. Listen to his story, go 
upstairs, and then sleep in your room. Then look at the map and go to 
the cave. Inside the cave go n, ne, nw and kill the mobs. Open the coffin 
once they're dead and 'free Sarkath khan' (10)
17) Rampart: fantasy/city portal/15e/exit/16e/2s/sinkhole.  Pray, 
accept_challenge, the answers are compassion, heart, mind, forgiveness, 
understanding, love.  Go out, and get back to the sinkhole.  Give soulgem 
to figure. (10)
18) NY Mugger: science/enter/u/2e/d/board train. When you get to NY 
wander around till you find the mugger and kick his fucking ass! (10)
19) Nightmare: chaos/enter/w/7n/w/n/search bed/sleep in bed.  Find the 
classroom (all e/all s). From there you need to get the following: box 
of chocolates (tray in cafeteria), art (art room), love letter 
(locker), binaca blast (principal), gift (bully's jacket pocket). Then go all 
n/e/s to your ideal mate. Give them all to her except the blast. Push 
button to get a minty breath. Kiss her (10)
20) Lothlarian: This has changed.  The only info I have for the new way 
is this: enter mirror/s/search trees/w/s/w/w/s/s/w kill the three 
Phoenix Guards then go north.  Kill general then search papers several times 
until is says something about the shrubs being the weak point of the 
defenses/e/n/search shrubs/n/e/n/e/e/s/s/s/skill ghost and enter fort.  
n/n/n/d/enter darkness kill arkhan and get standard.  
nw/u/s/s/out/n/n/n/n/w/w/s/w/s raise standard.  This will only work if you're evil. (10)
21) Gameshow: chaos/enter/2e/all n.  This one is random, and there are 
a few gameshows.  The ones it can be are price is right, wheel of 
fortune, and $10,000 pyramid.  To get to the pyramid you have to go to 
family feud, get to the final round, kill Richard Dawson and search wall. 
Price is right you just go in, kill bob barker, kill contestant, and spin 
the wheel.  Common answer on WoF is 'Cancer the tradesman', though this 
changes. (10)
22) Djinni: fantasy/city portal/all e/leave/all e/4n/2e/look at 
water/swim in ocean/ocean/look for the se corner or thereabouts.  You'll have 
to go east about 10 times before it puts you on an island.  Search sand 
until you find a bottle.  Open the bottle and you get sucked in, 
becoming a newbie with NOTHING until you finish it or leave.  Find the guard, 
kill him, get his stuff, and enter the palace.  Climb the stairs and 
find the Djinni.  Go back down, north.  Kill the guy and get the sword 
from him.  Go back upstairs and give it to the Djinni. (10)
23) Disney: find the mirror that has the small coastal town in it.  Go 
to the west until you can go south.  Then go all south and all west 
until you find Doc at the mine.  Say diamond and he'll give you a pickaxe.  
Swing pickaxe in every room of the mine until you find the diamond, 
then go back to where you went south.  Head all west to the house in the 
forest and go in.  Give the diamond to Snow White and say mirror.  
She'll give you a mirror, then go out and give the mirror to the old woman.  
She drops the award, pick it up and go back to the mirror.  Head south 
and check out the first house to the west.  Inside is Mickey, give the 
award to him. (10)
24) Destroy Barney: Chaos/enter/w/all s/all e/n.  This has been 
changed.  As soon as I figure it out... (10)
25) Arcanarton: Fantasy/road portal.  Go south and all west until you 
find an exit leading sw.  Go sw and you'll be at the tower.  Go up the 
tower to the very top, where you'll find Arcanarton.  Careful of the 
followers.  They're about 20k aggro and four in a room can hit you for 
over 200 points of damage in a single round.  Arcanarton is at the top, 
30k-35k, non-aggro, non-hunting wimpy safe.  Kill him.  There is also a 
marble here (see marble list for details). (10)
26) Perfection: Chaos/enter/4w/e/s/w/s/2e/n.  Enter warehouse/tease 
flower/kill tulip/kill nail/get everything/enter imperfect panel/kiss 
glass/lick film/ride particles/tease flower/enter imperfect 
panel/qwerty/lick film/ride particles/tussle flower/kill nail/kill tulip/get 
nothing/taste experience/conduct experiment/caress tulips/be perfect/do 
nothing/tease flower/enter perfect panel/up/enter heart/die/return 
nothing/somewhere/tussle flower/taste experience/climb ladder/return everything.  
You're on your own to get out.  I found that if you reverse some of the 
above steps you eventually get back out. (12)
28) Hobgoblin: Fantasy/city portal/12n/leave/all n.  Take the path and 
enter the cave.  Go all north once inside to the stream.  Jump over 
stream and search the bones. Go back and head west till you can go up.  Go 
up and kill the kid with knife.  Get the knife.  Go back down twice and 
head south to find the crazy hobgoblin.  Give the knife and the bone to 
him and he gives you a flute.  Go west and find the hobgoblin priest.  
Play flute and the priest will die. Get the amulet and leave.  Go back 
to the city portal and go 7 west and then south.  Search around near 
the Shrine to Zetron for the Tower of Zalusta.  Enter the tower, say 
Zalusta, go all up, go south and give the amulet to Zalusta. (15)
29) Alphabet: Chaos/enter/2e/d.  Kill the letters to spell the word 
HELICOPTER.  You only need one E.  Make sure you have one of the items 
other than a letter from one of the kills.  The letter R is in a hidden 
room.  Once you have all this, go back to the H room and 'spell 
helicopter'.  Note that if you leave the area for any reason before you spell 
helicopter that you have to do it all over again. (15)
30) Waldo: Chaos/enter/4w/2e/w.  You should be in Waldo's house.  Find 
the closet and search around.  You'll find a hole on the shelf.  Type 
'in' to go through it.  Walk like Waldo.  When you see the real Waldo, 
say waterworld and shake his hand. (20)
31) Frozen Dude: Fantasy/road portal/4e/7n/touch statue.  Find the 
lumberjack and kill him.  Grab his axe and wander into the forest there and 
chop tree.  Get the log and enter the cave.  Make sure to map it and be 
in verbose mode.  In one of the rooms with the dark hairy beast there's 
a dude frozen in the crystals if you search.  Light log and thaw dude.  
(20)
32) Free Stag: Go to Medlar (Fantasy/road portal/3e/4n) and find the 
throne room with the King and his guard.  Kill both of them and move 
stand.  Go down and kill the griffin.  Get the gem north of the griffin. 
(All these mobs are about 30k but can hit really hard).  From the king, 
go s/all e/u/w/s/e and kill the lady.  Get her gem.  Then go s/all w/all 
d/s/2e/s from the king. Kill the guard and get the key.  Go into the 
cell and kill the thief.  You should now have all 3 gems.  Go back to the 
courtyard and look around.  Find the gargoyle that says something about 
stones, and follow the order it lists otherwise you'll be seriously 
fucked (I mean it).  Go through the secret exit and follow the tunnel till 
you go up.  Go up and type 'free stag'.  (20)
33) Ebonbane: To enter barovia go from forest portal: s/s/sw/w/nw. 
Enter mist and wait for nightmare to appear. Kill nightmare/get 
phylactery/wear phylactery/in. Now you are outside of barovia. If you want back to 
the portal from here: enter the mist: go e and n (I think).  From mist 
go: n/nw/n/ne/n/nw. You are now at Barovia entrance.  From Barovia 
entrance go: n/ne/n/10w/s/3sw/6w/nw/2w/sw/as far w as you can. You will now 
stand in a cloak room. Go: n/e/search/get key/w/n/e/u/se/get key.  Then 
back to the cloak room. Then sw/2nw/w/s/get key/n/e/2s/w/s/kill 
spirit/deal with corpse/get key.  Back to cloak room and 2n/w/d/w. Simply 
arriving in the final room solves the quest. (20)
34) Dragon Egg: go the 1st level of the underdark, on the east side 
follow the passage south to the vortex that opens to the dragon area.  
Kill the guardian dragon, then go 
sw/2w/2n/w/s/w/s/w/n/w/n/w/2n/e/s/2e/n/w/3n/e/n/2e/s/e/n/2e. There you will fight The Guardian of the Future, 
Tiranor.  So named because he protects the dragon egg.  You'll have to 
kill him. He's over 1.5 million (Finger Windward.) Beat him down, 
somehow.  Now go east again, search the nest, get the egg. Run to the rabbit 
hole where Cae is and give him the egg. (20)
35) Whodunit: Chaos/enter/all e and turn south at Jag's.  Find the mist 
(exit1, exit2) and exit2. Go all s/e to the courtyard, then find the 
front door.  Search mat for the key and let yourself in.  Wander around 
inside and kill each mob in there except the butler and the ghost of 
Body.  Each person will have an item, and search each room until you find 
a weapon and a room item from each room with a mob in it.  There are 
some outside too (the rock in the courtyard, the dime in the fountain, 
and Mr. Grey in the Gazebo.)  The get all of these items and go to Body.  
Give him an item from a room, a person, and a weapon.  He'll tell you 
what's wrong.  Keep giving him items until you get it right. (25)
36) Spire: no info
37) Nuke: Science/enter/u/4n/d/2n/3e/6n/7e/3n/e/se and you'll be near 
an oasis.  Enter the oasis where you can and search. Kill the sludge.  
Search again and go down.  Go all east once inside and then south.  Kill 
the bandits and the soldier.  Search desk. Peruse papers. It should 
tell you where the test site is.  (this changes ALL the time. Make sure 
you're looking for the right one.) then go south and kill the soldier 
there.  Search his desk and get the key.  Find the secret door leading 
south in the main hall (should be before all the marked doors).  Search on 
the staircase for another key and unlock the next door.  In the next 
hallway there's a door leading north.  That's the computer room.  Go to 
the test site that you read about and search around for the passkey. 
When you get it go back to the computer room.  Look at the wall and the 
plug, then plug the computer in.  Insert passkey and then type the code.  
(I think you need to find the radio officer upstairs and take him!
!
 hostage to find the code). (25)
38) Haunted Manor: Fantasy/city portal/12n/leave/8n/w. Follow the path 
until it ends.  Find the window, and open shutter/open window/climb 
window then go s/e and go upstairs. Go w/n/examine ceiling/pull lever. Go 
2s and kill the guy and get dagger.  Go south again and smash amulet 
and kill the guy.  He summons imps, so run north and kill them before he 
summons enough to kill you. (25)
40) Attrition!: (25)
41) Van Richten: In Fantasy go s/sw/w/nw from forest portal and enter 
mist.  kill nightmare, get the phylactery and wear it.  Then go 
northward till you get past the sign and can go west.  go west till you find 
van rich, nod to him and go all w then e/s/4sw/8w/nw/n/3w/sw/2w/2n/steps, 
unlock door.  now you need a match: search jacket in main room, it's on 
the coat rack, get box of matches, and light match.  next you need the 
keys.  To get the first is look at stairs, look at banister, look at 
ball, move ball.  go east arch(maybe west, can't remember).  in one of 
the arches there are like 6 aggro dudes, but you can just stop combat on 
em, in study look at ashes, or search ashes, its in the fireplace.  
then go upstairs and then go westroom.  look at the drawer and move panel 
or something, then go door eastroom now you need the fetters.  open 
closet in spare bedroom and search closet, get bear.  go back to kitchen 
where the aggros are/were, go to pantrydoor
look at shelves, search shelves, move panel, reach into hole and you 
should get an axe.  leave immediately or a swarm of rats will attack you.  
then go to door3. immediately go stairs and unlock chest.  You should 
get the dress, then search pile/get shovel/unlock door/door/smash brick.  
an aggro 40k priest with 3 attacks comes out.  you need to get holy 
water and rites from him.  after he is dead and you get the stuff dig in 
this room and then room with ghost of a man, you should find a skull, if 
not you need to go back to the front door and go steps, dig there and 
the room north, when you find skull, ignore the skull for a bit, go back 
to child, with bear in hand, burn bear, then go back downstairs past 
the shadow and burn axe, then go to dining room and burn dress, then go 
back to skull and sprinkle water then SPEAK, must be speak, say won't 
work, the magic words are from 'peruse rites'.
42) Shadowrun: First: map Atlanta (in science) otherwise you'll get 
lost.
43) Katin: First find George Weathermay, but don't attack him. From 
forest portal, go: 2s, sw, w, nw, enter mist (to enter ravenloft) George 
Weathermay is in the forest south-west of barovia. So, once you've gone 
in, go:n,nw,n,ne,n,nw,n,ne,n,10w,s,4sw,6w... George hangs around here, 
particularly at the goblin camp just to the south. Mention the journal, 
and he gives it to you. Open it, and a key drops out. Get the key, and 
read the journal. Go back to forest portal.  From forest portal, go: 
3e, 5n, ne, search.  Follow the northern path to the hidden cemetery. In 
the northwestern part of the cemetery is a tomb. Enter the tomb, unlock 
the door. go down to the crypts. In the southern part of the crypts is 
a wight.  kill it and get the key it carries. Go to the northern wall 
of the crypts, where you'll find a door about 1/2 way along the wall. 
Unlock the door. Go north and kill the zombie lord. (30)
44) Hide And Seek: *Warning: you must have a 30 str when doing this 
quest!* Chaos/enter/3e/2s/2e/n/3e/n/2w/4n/enter.  Go 2e/3n/e and kill the 
brooms.  Search wall/move panel/bow down in worship/kill commander and 
get the jar.  2w/2n/u/2e/d and kill OJ, search plate, get the knife.  
E/enter/nw/2w/s and open dresser, wear ring, gaze into mirror/s/w and 
open refrigerator.  Go 2e and slide on slide/n/knock on door/kill 
vinnie/search bed/2d/s/kill tun-gai/e/kill Steve/search devices and get the 
toaster.  Then go w/n/2u/s/2e/se/2e/2n/e and open the refrigerator (if 
your strength is lower than 30 you won't be able to open it).  Go w/2n/u 
and search carpet.  Go nw, make sandwich, give sandwich to Joe and tag 
Matt.  (30)
45) Atlantis: Fantasy/road

50) Ravenloft2: Ok the first part of the quest is you have to kneel at 
donavich (assuming you know where donavich is, just ask if you don't) 
Get all the stuff. Then you have to find the gypsy in the forest west of 
Barovia.  Then at the gypsy kill the golem, and open the door. Don't 
nod to the gypsy, pray. She will port you to another area. Only one per 
reboot gets it. You are on your own. You also have a time limit: the 
hour-glass.  Go: enter/e/s/w/search organ/w/s/e/get 
invitation/w/n/e/e/n/w/w/ne/se/e.  Watch the wedding and killing until it says that you 
remember the relics and have to get them quickly before Strahd does.  Go: 
w/nw/sw/enter/e/e/e/e/get all Kill Strahd as fast as you can, then go all 
the way west and pray. (40)
51) Miyu: This is the only one I'm providing a map for. Look for a boy 
wandering around chaos.  look at him, type: trace symbol, and you're in 
the Miyu area.  Map of Kyoto: 
           *-*-*-*-T 
            |
     I     *
     |      | 
    *-A *
     |      | 		*=just a room
 *-*-*-*   	S=Start 
         |  | 		H=House entrance
        * *     * 	L=Library 
            |      | 	A=Armour 
           *-*-*-L 	T=temple 
            |		 I=Inn
H-*-*-*
            |
           * 
            | 
           *-S-*
The directions to this area take a while to get used to: they aren't n, 
s, e, w.  Instead it uses left, right, forwards, backwards, and the 
orientation depends totally from what direction you entered the room from. 
You'll get used to it. Go to H on the map. Search houses, enter house.  
Once inside house, search debris. You'll find a mirror, which the boy 
in the house will take. Kill boy, get mirror.  Also look at the picture 
on the wall here. Go out, and go to L on the map. Search the records, 
and you find a diary. Kill the boy here (he takes the diary before you 
can).Read the diary.. it gives some history to the quest.  Go to T.. 
this is where the vampire Miyu is. Go back one space from her. Drop all 
your gear.  Then go back into the temple. Say hi, and she asks if she can 
bite you. Say yes, then type: bite me.  She bites you, and reduces you 
to 1 hp.  When she bites you, she also makes you drop everything you 
were carrying, and she takes it. This is why you drop your stuff i!
!
n the other room. Heal yourself. get your gear, and then go to the 
Armor (marked A on map). Look at the mirror. Use mirror. Type: use mirror 
on armor. Then kill the armor.  This armor is tough... but you can't 
kill it at all unless you use the mirror on it first, and have been bitten 
by Miyu.  When Armor is dead, sever head from corpse. get head.  Go 
back to H, enter house, place head in picture. (40)

oil painting then enter it.  Enter cottage and request a story from the 
old woman.  Leave the painting and go back e/3s/2e and kill the thief.  
Go ne/n/e.  DO NOT GO DOWN. Kill the guards, search the rocks, and 
enter the cave. Go down and the Gnome Warlord is east (he's major trouble. 
Get help killing him).  Get the amulet from  his backpack. Go back to 
the oil painting and go north.  Move the grate and you end up in a maze.  
Map it.  By wearing the gnome's amulet most of the other gnomes will 
let you pass.  Kill the dragon and get the key, then go se and search 
dung.  Go d/3e/s/e/n/e/2s/3e/s/3w/s/2e/s/2w/s.  You can't go back north.  
Continue 3e/n/e/s/e and unlock the door, then go north and kill the

!
tle's throne room (2e from the oil painting).  Sit on throne and place

56) Cernunnos: Go to the Wayhaven library and look up Cernunnos and 
runes.  Go north and east of Wayhaven and find the druidic stones there 
(you'll be able to go up), in the center of the stones there's a stone, 
get the stone look at it and rub it. Kill this incarnation of Cernunnos 
- Cernunnos is the Celtic leader of the hunt.  Okay, now go to the 
Cernunnos area (east forest portal/e/4s/w/2s/w/s there's a priest 
somewhere down there.  Get into the forest and climb to the top of the hill 
(you'll notice the path you follow runs in a circle, keep trying to go 
directions into the circle to go up the hill).  To get out of the 
forest you'll have to find a path at the bottom of the hill that leads south 
back to the entrance, it'll be hidden as well. Go to the top of the 
hill, look at the runes on the stones you pass and try and make head or 
tales of them.  At the top of the hill you'll have to rub your stone 
again and fight an incarnation of Cernunnos, this time though you get a 
sword and helmet when you kill him.  Then you gotta figure out wtf the 
symbols mean and do something to finish the quest.  Don't try leaving the 
area.  After you rub the stone at the top of the hill the Hunt 
begins, and you'll be fighting tons of dumb mobs, hacknslash is 10/10. 
(40)

62) The Project: Enter Science, go all the way north through Houston 
and out into the wastelands then go: n, and about 5 or 6 w, then north 
into Nanook's desert area.  Go a couple north and west until you see a 
compound (it's a small area, so it won't take you long to find it).  
Enter the compound and then go all the way north to the shuttle to Mars.  
There is a messenger here that you can speak to. Ask him about Mars and 
mines and stuff. Go to the shuttle, enter it and go to Mars.  On Mars 
you're inside a large covered colony. Map it. The shuttle is in the most 
north eastern part of the colony. The areas aren't really very big, so 
it won't take you long to map it. From the shuttle, go:2 sw, w, sw, w, 
d, 2w, sw, nw, n, nw, n, ne, n, enter massage parlor. You can speak to 
the woman at the back by the stairs.  Go up the stairs and into a room 
with a woman in it. If she has a passcard then kill her and get it. If 
she doesn't then you'll need to look around on wandering workers fo!
!
r one.  Leave the massage parlor, go back s, sw, s, se, s, se, then go: 
sw, 2s, and into the large plaza area.  Wander around here until you 
find a tourist with a camcorder. Kill them and get it. You'll need the 
camcorder to record what you see down in the mines.  In the north east 
part of this plaza is the news office, where you'll need to take the info 
you get to solve the quest.  Find the secret genetics lab.  From where 
you entered on the shuttle, go: 2sw, w, nw, n, w, and use the elevator 
to go down. Wander about in the mines until you find a door with a card 
reader. You'll need to use the passcard that you got to open the door 
and enter the lab.  If you can't find the door in these mines, then try 
the mines on the surface of the planet. First buy an environment suit 
from the shop in the south east area of the plaza. If you leave the 
colony without it then you'll die. Wear the suit!  Then go to the airlock 
in the sw area of the plaza, and go out on to the surface of the p!
!
lanet. From here, go: 5w, 2n, e (hidden exit)and into the mines here. 
Once you enter the lab, immediately attack the scientist here(Dr. 
Gnolwright). Kill him. He'll summon orderlies to attack you, so if you have 
some sort of calming power then use it.  Once he's dead, then go east 
into his office. Search through the computer stuff. Search disks until 
you find one that looks important. Get disk.  Then go back west, n to a 
pit. Look at the pit full of bodies.  Start recording on the camcorder 
(the description tells you how).  Stop recording again. Then go back to 
the news woman in the plaza in the colony.  She'll immediately take the 
objects that you have. (55)
64) Ring of Power: Go to the zoo in chaos. From Da Void, it's n, w, n, 
and then search around a bit.. it's near the hide and seek quest. Enter 
the zoo, go 3n into zookeeper's house. Move the rug and get the key to 
open the drawer in his desk. Get the journal and read it all.  Go s, 
4w, s, sw, w, kill polar bear, get feather.  Go e, ne, 4n, enter tree, 
kill lion, get horn.  Leave the tree, go 2s, nw, w, kill panther, get 
tail.  Go e, se, s, enter house, kill zookeepers. Clean mirror, gaze 
mirror. You are transported to place with a maze. Now, make sure you have 
plenty of healing... lots of maze guardians that don't hit hard, but 
there can be lots of them. Also make sure you have something to mark your 
way through the maze or you will be terminally lost! Enter the maze. You 
will soon find that directions don't correspond: so that if you go left 
to get to one room, if you then go right you probably won't end up back 
where you began. So mark the rooms and work out the directions. !
!
There are 15 rooms total.  When I did it, the directions to the end 
were: forward, forward, left, left, backwards, left, left, backwards, 
left, left, forward, right, forward, and you should be at castle.  Don't 
enter the castle yet! Search stone, go down, kill dragon.  Put horn in 
conical hole, put feather in oblong hole, put tail in cylindrical hole, 
get ring of power.  Then go up. If you need healing go back, else enter 
castle, go up, kill wizard (he's fairly nasty, but not TOO bad), enter 
crack, melt ring in lava. (55)

69) Megatech: The new Megatech is a lot harder then the old one.  You 
have to go from the subway, u,4w,3s,all w, kill enforcers, n, 2w, n, 
kill enforcers open door, west, free man, and talk to him.  He'll give you 
a card and tell you about bob, now you go back to the subway, go 
u,5n,3e,5n,w,n,2w,4n then enter, and look at the stove, walls, and stuff.  It 
will tell you to turn one of them (it changes) or turn knob, or turn 
handle, but if you turn the wrong one, a hole will come.  If you enter 
the hole, you'll die.  You should find a down exit, go down and show the 
card you got from the man you freed and he will give you a bunch of 
passkeys.   Now, from level 300-450 you have to use the passkeys.  In each 
room you have to 'search', and in some you find a panel.  One should 
say just that it's black, but the one you want to find is the one that is 
long, and it has '[ready]' on it.  Now when you find the [ready], 
insert the lowest number of the passkeys you have (should get a 3,5,7!
!
,10) and so on.  On level 300, use passkey 3, and on level 350 use 
passkey 5 and such, this is the hard part.  Anyway, once inside, the 
directions are approximately: for level 50->100, all east, all s, should be 
like 3 or 5n, then go west.  For level 100->150 all east, all south, (sw 
corner) 2e,all north, e, n.  For level 150->200 w,n,6e,s,w.  For level 
200->250 2e,s,10w,10n,e,2sfor level 250->300 4n,e,s and all the levels 
after 300 you have to find the panel, and that's different for each 
person.  'search' in each room for them and you'll find panels in some.  
Look at panel and when you see a [ready] insert the correct passkey 
(lowest one that you have) check the numbers by look at front of passkey.  
On floor 500 go all west to Ancient Western dragon and kill it. Go west 
again and kill Arnold Hesler. (65)

72) Perplexus: OK, as the quest description says, go to Angelo, and 
look for the angel. From the west gate of Wayhaven (which is 12 west of 
the Wayhaven portal) go: 7n,14w,2s,bow (to Led), s, and you're in Angelo. 
Kill the guards on the main road here, and get the key. Go west, and 
into the guard outpost.  Kill the guards, search around, there's a 
trapdoor under the table. Move the table. unlock trapdoor, open, go down... 
follow the tunnels, killing cockroaches as you go. Where the tunnel 
forks, ignore the route to the troll, and go the other way (east). A few 
east, where the tunnel ends, you have to enter something or do something 
like that, and you'll find the angel. Speak to her.. use keywords like 
'hello', 'help', 'Perplexus'...and anything else that comes up. She'll 
tell you that to find out more, you have to speak to the old wise elf. 
And she'll tell you that he lives in the mountains to the north. If she 
still has it, she will give you a holy avenger sword (useful for k!
!
illing the evil elf king later).  Leave the tunnels, and back out onto 
the main road, while you're in town, have a look around: a couple south 
and one east of where you are, there's a statue of Perplexus... this is 
really Perplexus who has been turned to stone.  Go back west, and a 
couple south along the main road, until you can't go any further. There's 
a strange wall to the west.  'push wall' and you'll end up behind it. 
Go 3 west, 2s and enter the tower, or castle, or whatever. Go 2 east, 
3s, kill the 3 guards. Go 3 up, north, kill Goliath. Search painting, and 
you'll find a back room. There's Armor of the Dragon here (unbreakable, 
+3 strength), and 'quillions' which is part of the sword of Perplexus. 
Make sure you get this item! Go: out, s, 3d, 3n, 3w (back to tower 
entry). This time, go 2 west, 3s,m kill guards, 3u, n, kill Kargile. (this 
guy is a bit tougher than Goliath). Move plaque, and you'll enter a 
back room, this time you'll find the amulet of Perplexus.. keep thi!
!
s! To get back to town, go: out, 3d,3n,2e, leave,2n,4east. Head about 6 
north (until you can't go any further), and you'll be out of town. From 
here, you need to get to the northern mountains. The direct route, I 
think, is:7e,6n. Or, from the west gate of Wayhaven, it's: 3 west,12 
north, 4west, north.  Once you get to there, 'climb' twice. Go s, w, n, w, 
n, kill lich. The lich should have the handle for the sword.  Keep the 
handle!  Go s,e,directly south for a few...somewhere here you go 2d, 
kill golem, go n to cave kill Mamakin. 'enter gap' get the blade, and you 
have the 3 components for the sword!  DON'T make the sword yet!!!! As 
if you have to drop it or give it to someone, it vanishes, and the quest 
is ruined.  Go out, s,2u,n, go east as far as you can, until you find a

What you do is: from just inside palace, go: w, kill cleric (no wimpy,

cleric. He should vaporize with the first hit. Get out all 5 orbs, look 
at the stone, and insert orbs. When you do this, the queen is freed, 
and the quest is done! 
Notes: If you let the lich follow you any further than the base of the 
tower, then it will stop you leaving and you will have to fight it to 
the death. The liches take a while to kill, so they are annoying.  If 
you have somebody as a tank in the palace, don't wield the staff of the 
positive plane until you have to kill the final cleric. If you are 
wielding the staff then monsters will attack you, even if someone is trying 
to defend. (80)

are left behind. This is what you are looking for... so keep killing bats 
till you get some bat wings. If you're unlucky you may have to wander 
the forest for a bit, till you get some.  go: 2sw, 6w, 2s, nudge ismark, 
type: make helmet.  He'll now make you a bat wing helmet to w!

to help you get to said monster.
1) Enter fantasy portal, then go to the road portal.
2) Go into Balooga falls, 4 or 5 east of the portal I think, look for a 
bar to the north. go into the bar, and say forgers. (bar may be a 
little west or east...somewhere around the above directions is close).
3) Give 1000 coins to forger, he'll give you some I.D.
4) Go to the icy blue portal and get a ring or two of feather falling
5) Get the scroll of charm protection, I have no idea where it is, or 
if you can find a nice cleric who is quick enough at bouncing, they can 
kill the harpy without it (with a little luck and no lag)
6) Go west to the end of the road from road portal, north to the 
tundra, west a bit, look for a path leading north in the room descriptions, 
then go north.
7) Load the catapult with some junk, like bread, pull, and fire.  
You'll have to adjust it to fire it into the cave opening using adjust #, 
usually between 10 and 15.  When it is firing into the cave, load 
yourself in the catapult and get someone to fire you in there.  This is where 
the harpy is that will charm you.
8) Kill harpy, then kill the goblin king. sever head. take the head to 
the lord in the castle that is 3s and a couple west of the place where 
the road curves south...show I.D. to the keep guard, then enter. the 
lord is to the west or northwest.  Look around, find him, and give him 
the head. he'll give you some stuff, go back to the guild and collect the 
quest points.

Boomer Crisis

sewers.  Now, I don't know the way from here.. but the rats are VERY

ing killing guards as you go.  Just like Megatech,only some of the

Plain Text Attachment [ Download File | Save to Yahoo! Briefcase ] 

Qinfo (last updated 04/15/03)


The majority of these are written from memory so the exact syntax might 
not be included.  While there are directions for some of the quests, 
THERE ARE NO MAPS.  Those of us who did the quests on our own had to map 
and explore...SO SHALL YOU.  This is good for you because if you go 
through like a laundry list you WILL get popped for qinfo.  Special thanks 
to all the people who helped by providing information on quests I 
haven't done.  No names (for security reasons), but you know who you are.  
Whenever possible I've added notes about possible death traps and 
toughness of mobs.  

1) Marbles: these are found all over the mud. See Marble List. (1qp 
each)

2) Bbn Planet: chaos/2w/lift manhole cover/n/kill tech (5k)/search 
wall/kill tech (5k)/exa upper,middle, lower server/plug DCR.NET cable into 
one that is most alive (5)

3) Bug: No qinfo for this one.  The mosquito flies around pinnacle and 
everyone is free to attack it.  It can take massive amounts of damage, 
so dedicate some time for this.  It will randomly leave to another 
place in Pinnacle, and might just port you somewhere else randomly.  Only 
problem I can find is getting it after it's gone into the cemetery. (5)

4) Chop Tree: you need an axe and some patience for this one.  Search 
all the rooms in each of the mirrors with your trusty axe.  You'll find 
an old oak tree.  When you find it, just type 'chop tree' and you're 
done. (5)


5) Codename Kodiak: in newbie land, find the battletech mirror and go 
in. go nw/nw/e/search rubble/nw/nw/nw/search doors/nw and go into the 
elevator shaft. Go up and talk to the guy. Then, go back down into the 
elevator, and then search the boards. Go down and talk to the guy there, 
he'll give you a helmet. Wear the helmet and go 
u/se/se/se/se/w/se/sw/se/sw/and search trees. You'll see a hidden exit ONLY if you wear the 
helmet. Go kill Kodiak. (5)


6) Free Cho: chaos/enter/4w/e/s/e. you need to activate the machine by 
turn knob, flip switch, press button.  Kill all the mobs you see in 
there.  Careful, as this is no wimpy.  After you kill all of them, 
eventually you'll see Dr. Cho. Type 'free Cho', search beam to get out. Then 
you're done! (5)


7) Mack: newbie land. Newbie Mack: duploland:
1st- get ladder - 4w/4s/w/s/get ladder
2nd- get block #1 - buy donut/give to cop-(unlock door/open door/w/read 
wall(get number)) - go to bank/ask box (####)
3rd- get block #2 - enter barn/u/kill hen/search/give bone to dog 4th- 
kill mack-s end of house/l at ceiling/u/n/attach %% to %%/unlock 
door/open door/w (mack is kind of tough)

8) Newbie Academy: from newbie bin, go s, d, n and enroll in the 
school.  Answer all the questions, they answers are all in help files and 
room descriptions.  Make sure you know the phone number to the White 
House. If you aren't a newbie, you can still do this quest. In the sewers of 
Pinnacle look for the newbie mice and you're on your way, Science, 2w, 
3n, d, n, w, 2s, 3w, 2s, 2e, 5s, u. (5)

9) Ralintaro - search around (ground and brambles and wall) for 
skeletons.  One will have a scroll with magic words to get into the tower. 
Chant the words and enter and go e, exa peg/search peg, you'll find 
another scroll with directions to find a pen which is in the west most room.  
then go all north, west and kill the guardian then trace the symbol 
with pen and kill ralintaro. (5)

10) Resource Crisis: newbie land, find the mirror with the oil field in 
it. Search behind the seat of the truck. In the tool shed, in the 
office desk and just everywhere. You need a digital multimeter and a pair of 
wire clippers. Then, after you have those, find the tower you can climb 
up. There's a device. Test each wire with the multimeter.  The one with 
the charge is the one you need to clip. (5)

11) REMOVED

12) Tree: from cot: s/2e/2s/look at tree. (5)



13) Twelve Princesses:

chaos, 4w, e, s, w, s, 3e, enter, nw, recline.  Say hi, say king, say 
proclamation, say defenses, (if she doesn't give you the cloak now, 
drink the wine the first night then come back to her an say help), road, 
say hi, say yes, say daughters, say help, w, n, search each bed 
individually - search bed 1 etc - mine was bed 4. Go to your room, lay down, 
pour wine, wear cloak, go north, knock on bedpost, d, prune twig, w, prune 
twig, w, prune twig, board, search princesses, exa stopped couple, exa 
goblet, search goblet, clutch goblet, board, go back to king, give all 
twigs (in order) to king, give goblet to king.  Done. (8)


14) Arcanarton: Fantasy/road portal/2w/s/sw/trail/enter.  
Go up the tower to the very top, where you'll find Arcanarton.
 Arcanarton is at the top, 30k-35k, non-aggro, non-hunting wimpy safe.
  Kill him.  There is also a marble here (see marble list for details).
 (10)


15) Destroy Barney: Chaos/enter/w/3s/3e/n, enter.  kill the stagehand 
to get his pass, he moves around, so find him as you make your way 
towards barney. go e, 2n, search box, take liquor, 2w, 3s, 3w, show pass, 
search couch, give bottle to barney. (10)


16) Disney: find the mirror that has the small coastal town in it.  Go 
to the west until you can go south.  Then go all south and all west 
until you find Doc at the mine.  Say diamond and he'll give you a pickaxe.  
Swing pickaxe in every room of the mine until you find the diamond, 
then go back to where you went south.  Head all west to the house in the 
forest and go in.  Give the diamond to Snow White and say mirror.  
She'll give you a mirror.  Go all e from the beginning until you can swim, 
swim, go first s, kill ursula, s, get letter, go back to witch, show 
letter to witch, talk to witch until she says she wants the mirror, show 
mirror to witch, give mirror to witch.plan  She drops the award, pick it 
up and go back to the mirror.  Head south and check out the first house 
to the west.  Inside is Mickey, give the award to him. (10)


17) Djinni: Djinni Bring a light source.
Wayhaven, all e, leave, folow road e/ne until you get to the docks.  
In the room before either dock (exits e or n) swim or swim in ocean.
  Swim until you get to another beach with only exit south.  
Go s and then climb over rocks then examine cliff, examine 
cave etc.  Dive water, watch mob until it settles on the bottom, 
kill mob, examine bottom, search slime, get bottle.  
(Key you get from mob can be used to open a tan box on 
the island in this area to get a tan marble).

Once you 
have the bottle, return home or to a good area.  
You may want to put eq in a box as you can't use 
eq or guild powers once inside the bottle.
Remove cork.

You now suck.  I will only say the 
things you have to do - you may want to kill the
 mobs to get eq as you will have none.
Go to the room with Stinky/Skippy/whatever his name is
 - he is the newbie.  
Here you can pick flowers for a 100 hp heal.  
Left of him is a room with an anorexic slave.  
You can exa garden, pick vegetables, get vegetables.
Each vegetable gives approx 100 hp heal.  You will need these!
Go to the mage, wait until he says the magic word 'Kazam'  
To the right of the mage, search rocks for a hunting knife, 
this helps ALOT!  Go to centre and say key in front of a mob 
(I did this with the rogue but I assume it will work for any of them).
Mob will tell you which little mob in the outer circle has their 
particular key.
Go to them and say key again.  
They will give you a key to the door.
Kill guard in inner circle (I found him pretty hard), 
unlock door, go 2n - here is the mage (non-aggro)  
I would suggest having as many flowers/vegetables and ppl available 
for hmheal from afar as possible for this bit.
Kill mage, get sword. Go s, search room, say kazam, 
climb stairs, give sword to Djinni. (10)

18) Gameshow: chaos/enter/2e/all n.  This one is random, and there are 
a few gameshows.  The ones it can be are price is right, wheel of 
fortune, and $10,000 pyramid.  To get to the pyramid you have to go to 
family feud, get to the final round, kill Richard Dawson and search wall. 

Jepordy:  sw, e, e...buzz when question is asked.  Pat Sajak = weather 
man, Janice = Price is Right, Family Feud ABC --> CBS was in 1985.

Price is right you just go: n, kill contestant, join line, bid 450, e, 
kill Holly, take all, place blue tag on box, place green tag on beans, 
place red tag on package, 2e, kill contestant, kill bob, spin wheel. 

 Common answer on WoF is 'Cancer the tradesman, the locker clerk', 
though this changes. (10)

19) Nightmare: chaos/enter/w/7n/w/n/search bed/sleep in bed.  Find the

21) Orc Slayer: Go to Knivur (road portal, 4w, 2n, path) say orc

22) Rampart: fantasy/city portal/15e/exit/17e/2s/sinkhole.  Pray,

23) Sarkath Khan: fantasy/city portal/12n/leave/8n/5w/2n/path/enter.

34) Ebonbane: To enter barovia go from forest portal: s/s/sw/w/nw.

35) Free Stag: Go to Medlar (Fantasy/road portal/3e/4n) and find the

38) Accipiter: (25) 
Accipiter says: Ahh, good, good...you are most kind.  There is a 
special forest south of the mainland, the Forest of Types.  If only you'd be 
so kind as to retrieve for me a branch of the Moon Tree, and some 
Turquoise Jelly.     Accipiter says: Turquoise Jelly is a useful ooze 
congealed from the branch sap of a water tree. Some shamans value it in 
rain-making spells.  I myself use it in some recipes for its light,salty 
flavour.
Accipiter continues: It is a trifling request almost... both are easily 
enough obtained. And I will ensure that the forest will aid you.

Accipiter says: I need both items for a broth I am cooking.  When you 
return with them, we can both sit and enjoy the warm soup,and I'll tell 
you all you wish to know about the world of the creators.
Accipiter says: Oh, and concern yourself not with the crane who guards 
my home... he will pay you no heed.
Accipiter says: The Forest of Types is an enchanting island to the 
south,and a fairly new addition to our realms.  Its origins have a tale 
about them...
You say: tale
Accipiter says: Several centuries past, back when the realms were lush, 
untorn by the new beasts called into our lands whilst their summoners 
waged a bitter, pointless struggle, our kind was born.
Accipiter says: As it was told to our first generation, and as it has 
been passed down through our myths and blood, our own war would be with 
the man/trees of the north.  And yea, for centuries we did war with the 
trees, as it continues today thus.
Accipiter says: However, once a young hawk named Accipiter came of age, 
he decided that blood need not be spilt any longer, that our claws need 
not sunder bark, nor our beaks pierce the dry flesh of wood any more.
Accipiter says: This young hawk was the first to voice such a thought, 
and he was received thus with indifference at first.  However, he soon 
gained renown for his scholarship, and attained high rank among his 
kind despite his radical anti-war beliefs.
Accipiter says: And one day, this enterprising hawk embarked upon a 
certain project...he flew to an island south of Wayhaven;a desolate though 
fertile isle, and spent the greater part of the next forty years 
planting a magical forest ripe with all species of trees.
Accipiter says: When my creation was complete, I offered it to the 
man/trees as a gesture of peace, as a message that at least one man/bird 
remains averse to the violence of years past.
Accipiter says: And yea, once our Power gained word of my offering, I 
found myself here, on the cold ground, remanded to a fate of flightless 
impotency.  A bittersweet tale, yea

You say: hi
Cocodryllus says: Truly I am in no mood for pedestrian chat, 
adventurer. Begone, yea

You say: moon tree
Cocodryllus's right eye flashes.Cocodryllus says: It be the Moon Tree 
ye seek?  True, ye be close, as it lie just beyond this creek.  But to 
visit our fair Mother, I'm afraid, is quite out of the question.  You 
see, since with only one eye I cannot tell friend from foe, alas you may 
not pass.

You say: eye
Cocodryllus growls: My eye was snatched by the wicked serpent, Anguis.
You say: anguis
Cocodryllus says: Ah, we have a long history of enmity, he and I.  He 
is but a wee snake, ye see...but he caught me unawares last night, and 
plucked my eye from my brainpan.
Cocodryllus says: He slithered off before I could lay chase.  He is 
probably back in his rocky refuge by now.
Cocodryllus says: I wonder how he even made it to this isle.  Perhaps 
he stowed away in some adventurer's boat.
You say: rocky
You say: refuge
Cocodryllus snarls: The piteous beast finds home in brief rock 
settlements, and prefers unbearably hot, dry conditions. Indeed, he is not a 
native of this island.

Charter forest of types at the ferry.

44) Katin: First find George Weathermay, but don't attack him. From 
forest portal, go: 2s, sw, w, nw, enter mist (to enter ravenloft) George 
Weathermay is in the forest south-west of barovia. So, once you've gone 
in, go:n,nw,n,ne,n,nw,n,ne,n,10w,s,4sw,6w... George hangs around here, 
particularly at the goblin camp just to the south. Mention the journal, 
and he gives it to you. Open it, and a key drops out. Get the key, and 
read the journal. Go back to forest portal.  From forest portal, go: 
3e, 5n, ne, search.  Follow the northern path to the hidden cemetery. In 
the northwestern part of the cemetery is a tomb. Enter the tomb, unlock 
the door. go down to the crypts. In the southern part of the crypts is 
a wight.  kill it and get the key it carries. Go to the northern wall 
of the crypts, where you'll find a door about 1/2 way along the wall. 
Unlock the door. Go north and kill Tireena (12k). (25)

46) Nuke: You read the documents carefully, and discover that the test 
site is just north of Detroit. Wass spills his guts and tells you he 
hid the keycard at the test site in the tent.

Wass mumbles: We'll show em...fire that nuke...
He also tells you that the code for the launch is "10.22.74"
Science/enter/u/4n/d/9n/8e/se and you'll be near an oasis.  Enter the 
oasis where you can and search. Kill the sludge.  Search again and go 
down.  Go all east once inside and then south.  Kill the bandits and the 
soldier.  Search desk. Peruse papers. It should tell you where the test 
site is.  (this changes ALL the time. Make sure you're looking for the 
right one.) then go south and kill the soldier there.  Search his desk 
and get the key.  Go to the doors in the eastern hallway and enter the 
middle one.  Take the soldier hostage and he'll tell you where he hid 
the keycard.  Find the secret door leading south in the main hall 
(should be before all the marked doors and is listed in the long room 
description).  Search on the staircase for another key and unlock the next 
door.  In the next hallway there's a door leading north.  That's the 
computer room.  Go to the test site that you read about and search around 
for the passkey (sit on hole to find it). When you get it go back to the 
computer room.  Look at the wall and the plug, then plug the computer 
in.  Insert passkey and then type the code.  (I think you need to find 
the radio officer upstairs and take him! hostage to find the code). (25)

47) Spire: First go to wforest, 1e, 2s and talk to grus.  Talk to him 
about war etc and eventually ask him about spoils.  He'll give you a 
cube. In the tundra in northern fantasy is a room (5 or 6s, 5 or 6 e of 
portal ice) where there is a 'shadow' in the room descrip.  Exa or search 
the shadow and you get the spire before you.  Enter spire.  Be sure to 
exa/search lotsa stuff in this area. Map the spire out real quick, be 
sure not to 'get' anything yet.  This could get you stuck. Do not attack 
stuff until the thing at the end, you don't need to.  Ok, from the base 
go up once, search the walls, etc. here and you'll find a piece of 
bark, get bark, it falls, you see symbols on the step, exa them, and write 
them down.  In the room with the bird/man, talk to him, he will 
eventually start looking down at a lever, but he is too prideful to ask you 
for help, pull the lever, you get knocked into the se corner.  Search 
around in here, you get a piece of paper that tells you how to enter the 
room behind the tar-door-circle thingy.  In the room with the man being 
turned into a plant, trace the symbols you found on the step into the 
blood and he will spell out 'VOLUNTEER'.  In the room with the machine 
and skeleton you can find a pipe on the machine.  Put the cube in the 
pipe, it runs, and then you can get the plant from the skeleton's chest.  
In a room just up and east from the tar-door, a plant loads on the 
floor.  After you go through the tar-door and talk to the guy in here for a 
long while, you will find his name to be Michael.  After this you can 
go and get the plant, a guy will walk in, and he won't let you go out 
until you give the name of the plants father (michael).  As you have 
learned Michael wants his daughters back.  Give the 2 plants to him.  He 
will then say you have his protection in the Spire.  Go all the way to 
the top.  Here, simply 'volunteer'.  After a long wait you will be in the 
room with a thing with name = the symbols you saw earlier.  Bow to 
thing.  Should be done. (25)

48) Whodunit: Chaos/enter/3s/all south/out2/s.  Go all s/e to the 
courtyard, then find the front door.  Search mat for the key and let 
yourself in.  Wander around inside and kill each mob in there except the 
butler and the ghost of Body.  Each person will have an item, and search 
each room until you find a weapon and a room item from each room with a 
mob in it (some rooms only have 2 items in it).  There are some outside 
too (the rock in the courtyard, the dime in the fountain, and Mr. Grey 
and a gun in the Gazebo.)  The get all of these items and go to Body.  
There is also a swithblade hidden in one of the secret passages in the 
corner rooms of the house ("search" to find them). Give Ghost an item 
from a room, a person, and a weapon.  He'll tell you what's wrong.  Keep 
giving him items until you get it right. (25)

with the quest, but nice).  Go kill a peace and give Green the feather.  
He'll tell you to ask the paragons about Blue.  Wander around saying hi 
to every Paragon you see.  Eventually one will tell you what it saw and 
give you Hope.  Give Hope to Silver and ask him about all the players 
again.  Go talk to Gold (3e, 3s from silver), say help, he'll tell you 
to go see Bronze (from Gold: 4e, 9n, ne, climb, all up).  Wait at the 
top for Bronze to show up (will take a minute or 2).  Say help.  Bronze 
will ask you to go kill Grey (From Bronze, all down, sw, 6s, 3e, n, 
enter, all d.  Kill Grey and head back to Bronze.  He'll take you on a 
flight to see Blue and give you proof.  Return to Silver and give him 
proof.  Talk to him and agree to help him kill black.  Go 19e, 3s, kill 
guard, se, kill guard, sw, kill guard, enter, kill Black (let silver tank).

55) Shadowrun: First: map Atlanta (in science) otherwise you'll get 
lost.

Find Mr Johnson in Atlanta.  He is located 2w, 2n, 2w from the subway 
entrance.

Speak to him about the quest, then follow these steps:

1. First, get the door remover in the gunshop on the south end of Avery 
Street by killing the guy in the 2nd room. (subway, 1w, 9s, 2w).

2. Activate the remover in the activator 5n and 4e, d from the subway 
entrance.

3. Go to the green lightning gang hideout (1w, 7s, 3e, s) and remove 
the door that is 2 south and up from the entrance.  Kill the leader for 
the passcard. He is 47k, but only has one attack.

4. Activate the passcard in the activator in the north east corner of 
town.  From the subway, 4n, 6e, 2n, e, s.

5. The go down to the parking garage (2e, n from subway) and go down to 
the 5th sublevel. In the northwest corner of the 5th level insert 
passcard.

6. Enter and kill the drone.  It will die easily.  Go past it and get 
the datachip.  Then get out of the garage.  

7. Go and activate the datachip in the 3rd activator, which you have 
not used yet.  It is located 7e from the subway.  Then go and give the 
activated datachip to Mr. Johnson in the bar in the northwest part of 
town.

8. He will give you 10k coins and the qps.. (30)

65) Miyu: This is the only one I'm providing a map for. Look for a boy 
wandering around chaos.  look at him, type: trace symbol, and you're in 
the Miyu area.

The directions to this area take a while to get used to: they aren't n, 
s, e, w.  Instead it uses left, right, forwards, backwards, and the 
orientation depends totally from what direction you entered the room from. 
You'll get used to it. Go to H on the map. Search houses, enter house.  
Once inside house, search debris. You'll find a mirror, which the boy 
in the house will take. Kill boy, get mirror.  Also look at the picture 
on the wall here. Go out, and go to L on the map. Search the records, 
and you find a diary. Kill the boy here (he takes the diary before you 
can).Read the diary.. it gives some history to the quest.  Go to T.. 
this is where the vampire Miyu is. Go back one space from her. Drop all 
your gear.  Then go back into the temple. Say hi, and she asks if she can 
bite you. Say yes, then type: bite me.  She bites you, and reduces you 
to 1 hp.  When she bites you, she also makes you drop everything you 
were carrying, and she takes it. This is why you drop your stuff in the 
other room. Heal yourself. get your gear, and then go to the Armor 
(marked A on map). Look at the mirror. Use mirror. Type: use mirror on 
armor. Then kill the armor.  This armor is tough... but you can't kill it at

where you began. So mark the rooms and work out the directions. There 
are 15 rooms total.  When I did it, the directions to the end were:

area of the plaza. If you leave the colony without it then you'll die.

go out on to the surface of the planet. From here, go: 5w, 2n, e

attack the scientist here(Dr. Gnolwright - he is no leave, 50k)). Kill 
him. He'll summon orderlies to attack you, so if you have some sort of 
calming power then use it.  Once he's dead, then go east into his office. 
Search through the computer stuff. Search disks until you find one that 
looks important. Get disk.  Then go back west, n to a pit. Look at the 
pit full of bodies.  Start recording on the camcorder (the description 
tells you how).  Stop recording again. Then go back to the news woman 
in the plaza in the colony.  She'll immediately take the objects that 
you have. (55)

82) Perplexus: OK, as the quest description says, go to Angelo, and 
look for the angel. From the west gate of Wayhaven (which is 12 west of 
the Wayhaven portal) go: 7n,14w,2s,bow (to Led), s, and you're in Angelo. 
Kill the guards on the main road here, and get the key. Go west, and 
into the guard outpost.  Kill the guards, search around, there's a 
trapdoor under the table. Move the table. unlock trapdoor, open, go down... 
follow the tunnels, killing cockroaches as you go. Where the tunnel 
forks, ignore the route to the troll, and go the other way (east). A few 
east, where the tunnel ends, you have to enter something or do something 
like that, and you'll find the angel. Speak to her.. use keywords like 
'hello', 'help', 'Perplexus'...and anything else that comes up. She'll 
tell you that to find out more, you have to speak to the old wise elf. 
And she'll tell you that he lives in the mountains to the north. If she 
still has it, she will give you a holy avenger sword (useful for 
killing the evil elf king later).  Leave the tunnels, and back out onto the 
main road, while you're in town, have a look around: a couple south and 
one east of where you are, there's a statue of Perplexus... this is 
really Perplexus who has been turned to stone.  Go back west, and a couple 
south along the main road, until you can't go any further. There's a 
strange wall to the west.  'push wall' and you'll end up behind it. Go 3 
west, 2s and enter the tower, or castle, or whatever. Go 2 east, 3s, 
kill the 3 guards. Go 3 up, north, kill Goliath. Search painting, and 
you'll find a back room. There's Armor of the Dragon here (unbreakable, +3 
strength), and 'quillions' which is part of the sword of Perplexus. 
Make sure you get this item! Go: out, s, 3d, 3n, 3w (back to tower entry). 
This time, go 2 west, 3s,m kill guards, 3u, n, kill Kargile. (this guy 
is a bit tougher than Goliath). Move plaque, and you'll enter a back 
room, this time you'll find the amulet of Perplexus.. keep this! To get 
back to town, go: out, 3d,3n,2e, leave,2n,4east. Head about 6 north 
(until you can't go any further), and you'll be out of town. From here, you 
need to get to the northern mountains. The direct route, I think, 
is:7e,6n. Or, from the west gate of Wayhaven, it's: 3 west,12 north, 4west, 
north.  Once you get to there, 'climb' twice. Go s, w, n, w, n, kill 
lich. The lich should have the handle for the sword.  Keep the handle!  
Go s,e,directly south for a few...somewhere here you go 2d, kill golem, 
go n to cave kill Mamakin. 'enter gap' get the blade, and you have the 
3 components for the sword!  DON'T make the sword yet!!!! As if you 
have to drop it or give it to someone, it vanishes, and the quest is 
ruined.  Go out, s,2u,n, go east as far as you can, until you find a tree... 
climb rope., e, u, and speak to Elistan, who will tell you more info 
about where the wise elf is. If you're not carrying the holy avenger 
sword, that the angel had, then he won't tell you much, but that's OK. Go 
2e,2d.  There's a bedroom to the south. Look at the dresser.. there are 
5 drawers.  Search all the drawers (search drawer1, search drawer 2 
etc.). You should find a diary (read this.. gives you more info) and a 
key.  Go north out of the bedroom again. There's a door in the floor: open 
door and go down. Go west and speak to the queen (don't remember her 
name) she'll tell you a little more about where the wise elf lives, and 
also tell you to ignore any messages saying he's not in.  Go west, n,d, 
out,w,4s,about 15 east, till there's a house to the north.  Go north. 
There's a sign saying that the wise one's out... ignore this and unlock 
gate (with the key from the dresser) enter the house. kill the guards, 
go north to an empty room. search fireplace, move brick, get crystal. 
Touch crystal (must be in this room), and the wise elf (Yeltor) will 
appear. He'll tell you what to do for the quest, if you talk to him.  He 
tells you to go see the scout in the village. Leave by going south a few 
times, and you'll end up back at the main path. Go back about 2 west, 
till there's a road to the south. Go south, east, ring bell, and the 
scout will come. say help, say quest, and he'll ask you who sent you... 
say 'Yeltor' Then he'll ask you to show him an item of Perplexus... show 
him the amulet.  He'll tell you to nod when you're ready. Now this is 
the good bit: only one person is supposed to be able to get into the 
gray elves tree at a time... but once he's been shown the amulet, anybody 
can 'nod' and be allowed entry. So you can take a tank with you, to 
fight the creatures you have to fight.  nod, and you'll be escorted into 
the back room. Go d, 2e,ne,4e,u,e (kill, or ignore the gray elves along 
the way). You're at the entry to the gray elves' tree. As mentioned in 
Elistan's diary, there's some twigs by the door. (look at the panels to 
the left and right of the door).  Now, if you get the combo wrong, then 
you may be roped up by your feet, and you need a knife of some sort 
from one of the monsters in the area to cut the rope, otherwise the only 
way out is to quit.  If this happens, you lose everything. So: before 
you try the combo, drop all your gear! Especially the quest items. If you 
get strung up  then you can quit but you have to come back and start 
over again.  If the door opens, and you don't get roped up, then get all 
your gear, and enter the tree. Go east, to a major intersection of 
tunnels. Now according to Elistan's diary, you have to put something in a 
large bowl, to open another door. From the intersection, go se, and 
follow it south. Search rags and you'll find an elf.  talk to him a bit 
using key words.  he'll reveal that if you place a stone in a bowl to the 
south, then you can take a rock from a room to the north, and drop it 
(he doesn't say where to drop it). Go back to the major intersection of 
tunnels. This time go ne, east for a few. There's a set of tunnels 
forking off: ne,e,se In each of these rooms is a priest. In each case, kill 
the priest, search the altar, and get the precious stone. You should 
have a ruby, and emerald, and a sapphire. Go back west, sw, to the major 
intersection. There is possibly a trap to the south, so drop your gear 
here. Just take the ruby with you. This time take the south corridor... 
look at markings on the wall. They will show what gem has to go in what 
bowl. Go north.. if you have done the bowl bit wrong, you'll fall into 
a pit and have to quit. Go north.. collect your gear. Go about 3 north, 
to the end of the corridor. Kill the skull. Go west: a room on some 
sort of springs... interesting, but you don't know what to do... Go back 2 
east, a room with a rock in it. Now that the ruby's in the bowl, and 
you have both other gems in your hands... you should be able to lift the 
rock. Go back to west to the springy room. Make sure both you and your 
tank are in the room. drop the roc and! the spring floor will drop, and 
deposit you in another room. Go west, kill the priests. Look at 
fountain. look at skull. Swivel skull. A secret door opens to the south. Go 
south, and kill the gray elf king. Make sure you have a tank!  Get the 
cloak of Perplexus! Go back north.. l at altar, search altar.  press 
switch until a portal opens up. Enter it, and you're back on the trail in 
the forest, north east of where the scout is. Go back west as far as you 
can, then go back east one. Go 4 north, east, in, 
u,s,2u,2w,d,w,d,2w,n,2d (out of the mountains) Go back to Angelo: from here, it should be: 
6s,7w,2s,bow,3s,e. here, or around here, is the statue of Perplexus... 
Holding the 3 pieces of the sword: handle, blade, and quillions, type: 
make sword, and the ego sword is made. type: place sword. type: place 
cloak type: place amulet and, the statue will come to life. (75)

83) Pyron: (75)

84) Dragon Knight: Go to the Portal of Life. From forest portal it's: 
3w, 2sw, 2s, 2e.Good luck trying to map it.  The area is dotted with 
following wyverns, which aren't hard to kill.  Object: free the queen from 
being entombed in stone. To do this you need 5 colored orbs that you 
get from killing the dragon knights, and the Staff of the Positive Plane 
to kill the High Cleric who guards her. You also need a hexagonal key 
and an octagonal key to get to her.  OK, go to green keep, kill guards 
(easy), n, e, search hearth, get rusty key,w, n, ne, 2u, n, push stone 
(on pillar), get red key. Ignore all other items here.  Go to blue keep, 
kill guards, n, w, search hearth, unlock door (with rusty key), hearth, 
search look at brick, l at symbols, push stone/button, get green key.  
Go back to green keep, 2n, nw, 2u, unlock door with green key, n, there 
is a dragon knight here. Wait for a minute and he will turn into a 
green dragon and attack. Kill him (he's not too hard). Get the green orb.  
Never wimpy from a dragon knight or demons come and attack you, and 
they are annoying.  Go to the 'wiz tree'. There is something in the 
description about an odd tree here. Search, turn knob, enter, u, and you will 
see an elven wizard. Say help, and he will give you a rainbow amulet. 
Wear this.  Go to red stronghold. kill guards, 2n, ne, 2u, n, make sure 
you're wearing the rainbow amulet, and enter. Make sure nobody follows 
you in.  There is a pillar here. Push stone, get blue key.  Leave the 
room and go down, sw. This time go nw, 2u, unlock door with red key, n, 
wait till dragon knight turns into dragon, kill him, get red orb. Go to 
blue keep again, 2n, nw, 2u, unlock door with blue key, n, and there is 
a bench here. Lay on bench, dragon knight comes, kill blue dragon, get 
blue orb. Go to village.  Follow the path into the center of the 
village, and then the wise woman is off to the nw. Go to her, and say help.  
She will give you a torch.  Leave the village and go to white keep. 
Kill guards, 2n and you see a fountain.  Melt ice (need that torch). Get 
scroll. Go ne, 2u, n, push stone (on pillar) and get black key. Go to 
black keep. Kill guards, 2n, nw, 2u, unlock door with black key, n, kill 
black dragon knight, get black orb.  Go s, 2d, ne, 2u, n, kill cleric. 
Push stone (on pillar). get white key.  If you enter the doorway here 
you will go straight back to white keep. Go to white keep, 2n, nw, 2u, 
unlock door with white key, n, kill dragon knight, and get white orb. 
OK, now you should have all the dragon orbs!  You need the more keys and 
the staff: Go to wyvern nest, climb (up into nest).  Kill all 4 
wyverns, search nest and you should find the staff of the positive plane. If 
not, go searching around the cliffs for more nests. You can insert one 
of the orbs into the staff, but don't try this right now, because you'll 
lose the orb and will have to go get another.  Go to lizard nest. Climb 
up, kill faerie lizards, search nest and you should find a crystal key. 
If not search around for more nests.

Hexagonal Key: Go to place marked Temple on map, search bushes, enter, 
look at murals, move brick, get hexagonal key.

Octagonal Key: The octagonal key is on a courier who wanders in the 
area.  I have always found him in the north east section.  Follow him and 
kill him (easy). Get octagonal key. 

When you're ready for the final assault on the palace, look at the 
scroll. Chant the words on the scroll and you end up at the cliff where you 
have to 'search cliff' and go up. Actually, this place is 7n of the 
portal of life, and you don't need the scroll at all to get there.  Go up, 
n, kill lich, 2 or 3n, till you see a pillar. Unlock pillar (with 
crystal key) and the drawbridge comes down. Go north and into palace.  The 
palace is basically a square, with a tower at each corner. In each tower 
is a device you need to unlock (using hex or octagonal key). When this 
happens the pyramid they were supporting floats to the ground and you 
can go in to free the queen.

What you do is: from just inside palace, go: w, kill cleric (no wimpy, 
but he's not too hard), sw, up, kill lich, (no wimpy), u, unlock 
device. 2d, ne, 2e, kill cleric (no wimpy), se, up, now there is a lich here 
who won't let you go up. Kill him, and you can go 2u, unlock device, 
2d, kill lich, nw, 2n, kill cleric (no wimpy), ne, u, dispose of the 
lich, u, unlock device, 2d, sw, 2w (past a couple of clerics, but they 
allow you to wimpy), nw, u, dispose of lich, u, unlock device. Now all the 
devices are inactivated, and the pyramid should come down. Go 2d, se, 
e, kill the 2 clerics, 2s, wield the staff of the positive plane, kill 
cleric. He should vaporize with the first hit. Get out all 5 orbs, look 
at the stone, and insert orbs. When you do this, the queen is freed, 
and the quest is done! 

Notes: If you let the lich follow you any further than the base of the 
tower, then it will stop you leaving and you will have to fight it to 
the death. The liches take a while to kill, so they are annoying.  If 
you have somebody as a tank in the palace, don't wield the staff of the 
positive plane until you have to kill the final cleric. If you are 
wielding the staff then monsters will attack you, even if someone is trying 
to defend. (80)

88) Balooga Falls: Note: You'll need an anchor.  Go to the bridge and 
knock out the pegs, then grab or hold rope before you knock them out.  
Go to nyrow. say hi, quest, demons, jobs, angeldemons.  4w/n/e/n/look at 
painting/look at bench/open bench/get map/look at map.  The go s/say

just pray. Kill Lars treetop, get all. n/3e/4n/wade into water or wade 
into river. climb into barrel (you'll get that from Lars).  Here is the 
"quest" part. (look at everything just to play dumb) n/3e, walk between 
poles. n kill demon (not so hard, 20K I think) Break mirror, n/get

n/w , say gnos and you'll get hit by water, so you lose ALL HP except

Turn your "panic buttons" back on and go e/n/step into light. Go n/w kill

get the wrong answer), notice the name he says... like "Say hi to blah 
for me", and notice his name.) 2n/w, get parchment, look at parchment.. 
(You should do this before anything else) and then afterwards go get 
the mirror gem and such. search throne, search hand, arm, search left arm 
rest (and right arm rest) open one of them (I think it was the right), 
and get gem (4). Go e/2n/ne/e look at skull, look at balls. throw balls 
at skull. You now get gem 5. Go w/n/nw/w/avert eyes from cage, pull 
rope, kill gorgon get amm (gem 6) e/n. Say hi, gems demons, gnos, 
angeldemons. You should go to this guy first too, (after stilts and parchment 
because he gives you lots of good information, about the room of the 
kings (throne room). Ok.... Right n is a DEATHTRAP... To avoid it, you 
should type pray to gnos every round.. He will save you.. BUT if you are 
lagging... R.I.P. My advice is to trigger this to go every round. 
Search/get all (gem7)/n/say hi, he will say "I don't talk to strangers". 
Remember the name at the riddle dude, say Byro n.. He will ask who told 
you, say Ragorse. Then to let him pass, say false god or quest or 
something. Right n is a VERY DANGEROUS Hydra, class 120K or something. You have

and back s to the manticore, and then n again, hopefully he will let 
you pass. If not you have to kill him. Go n until you come to a door, 
search it and search holes. Here is the right sequence you should put the 
gems in. If not it's been changed: Hole 7=Emerald. Hole 6=Ruby. Hole 
5=Sapphire. Hole 4=Diamond. Hole 3=Pearl. Hole 2=Opal. Hole 1=Topaz. Go

demons. look at staff. You will notice its base is "screwed" (the hole in the

89) Wayhaven: First: map all of Wayhaven.  
From the portal go: 5e/5s/e and climb stairs to the clerk.  
Present yourself and he'll tell you that you need citizenship.
Enter the stall n/w of portal and buy a guitar.  
Then go to the woman on balcony (6n/2e of portal).  
Serenade woman and receive her message.  
Find the captain of the guard (4s/climb staircase from portal) and 
deliver message.
He'll give you another message.  
Go back to the woman and deliver the new message.  
She gives you a note, take this to the guild master 
(e/2n/w/enter door/w/present note from woman).  
He gives you guild sponsorship.  
Go back to the clerk and present yourself.  
He tells you to get a bounty hunter's license.  
Go to tintorillos (w/s of clerk) and 'prepare document'.
They'll tell you that you need ink and notarized paper.  
Go to the ink shop (n/w/5n/7e/2n/2e/3n/4w/2n/e from tintorillos).  
Ink master tells you that you need an ink fish 
(w/n/4w/s/kill fisherogre/get rod/catch fish).  
Go back to ink master and buy ink.  
Go to the paper shop (w/n/3w/4n from ink shop) and buy legal bond 
paper.
Go get it notarized (3w/2 or 3s from clerk).  
There's a sign saying that the notary office is along the Promenade.
You can't get there unless you have a pass so go to the printer shop
(12e/2n/2e/2n/w from portal) and buy pass.  
He'll tell you to go to a forger and 'shimmy on out of here'. 
Shimmy and you'll go up a ladder to the forger.  
He needs special and ink and paper so guess where you get to go again!  
Come back and get your pass.  Go back to the Promenade 
(5e/5s/w/3s/3e from portal) and 'notarize document'.  
Go e/n search the dock.  Leap to the boat you find, 
free smuggler and he'll take you back and give you an important item.
Go back to tintorillos (see why you need to map Wayhaven??) 
and 'prepare document' by going s of the clerk and typing 'sign 
document'.
The 5 councilors each need a bribe, and each bribe is different.  
1: a gem (dwarven traders north of portal), 
2) a gladhand (hustler in se section of Wayhaven), 
3) a book on making money 
(Wayhaven library: 7w/3s/2e/2s/u/w from portal. 
Kill everyone, search the shelves and steal book), 
4) a drow tapestry (go to gunpowder shop [s/3e/n of paper shop] and buy 
gunpowder.
Go to the citadel cannon [4s/2w/3s of portal], light cannon, and climb 
in cannon.
Go through the citadel and kill the guards.  
Kill the captain and step in haze.  
Kill the guards, climb up, kill more guards, and go west. 
Kill the guards, but not the sergeants.  
Keep heading west, kill the captain, and go west and then north.  
Search a few rooms north and get the tapestry.  Give it to the 
councilor), 
5: silver dragon scale (challenge arena [4n/e/d from portal] 
and challenge the baby silver dragon.  
Kill it and get the scale.)  
Once you have all 5 signatures go back to the clerk and present 
yourself.
He tells you about the quest.  
Head to the brothel (8e/3s/3e/2n/e from portal).  
Peruse the book and request a whore.  
You need to go the guild HQ (8n/5e/2n/e from portal) and request guild 
membership.
Buy thread and velvet from the stalls in the bazaar (s/w and s/e from 
portal) 
and go to the seamstress (12e/2n/2e/7n from portal) where you order a 
sash.  
Go back to the brothel, order a whore, and pleasure him/her.  
Request the madam and kill her.  She escapes through a secret door.  
Search around, go through the secret door, kill her, get the papers and 
the key.  
Search around to find the exit again.  
Now, go to the chief mugger in the mews (5e/4n/e/3s/e from portal) 
and kill the mugger (who has a dwarf mask).  
Go w/3n/4w/s/e/s and wear the mask to go into the dwarven pub.  
Kill the 5 dwarves that attack you and search the mirror and go down 
through the trap door.  Then go n/e and search around.  
Open the door you find with the key you got from the madam.  
Kill the chief mugger who attacks (80k) and then search around to get 
his seal.  
You also find a secret exit leading you out to a safe place.  
Go back to the clerk and present yourself again.  
As you head to the mayor's office you fall into a well.  
Blow the whistle you got from the smuggler and he'll come and take you 
to a 
secret entrance.  Search the ladder (to disarm a trap).  
Climb up and kill the mayor. (95)

73) Vole the Hateful: REMOVED 

Go to Deep Mountain and find the drow translator.  Go to level 4 of the 
underdark maze and get the maul of the titans.  Go to the 'open fields' 
and 'dig' 20 or 30 times in each room until you hear a rumbling sound.  
It will say you fell into a hole or something, dig until it says you 
can't anymore.  Listen to what you're told and you'll be given a strand 
of beads.  Hang on to this!  Go back to level 4 of the maze and listen 
at the dusty corner until you hear someone mumble something.  Make a 
note of what word is mumbled.  Go to the demon spider and kill it.  Search 
the throne and open door, go down and search around.  You'll be asked 
for a password (this is the word you heard mumbled).  Keep going and 
head south at the first intersection you run into.  Break beads and watch 
the show.  Note: be VERY careful of the demon spider.  If you're lucky 
you'll get the demon spider carapace from it (a nice piece of armor). 
(80)
